Use the new key name if it's in the mapping, otherwise keep the old one\n            new_key = key_mappings.get(key, key)\n            new_item[new_key] = value\n        renamed_data.append(new_item)\n    return renamed_data\n\n# Example usage\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    # Sample data simulating records that might come from an API\n    sample_json_data = [\n        {\"id\": 1, \"oldName\": \"Alice\", \"currentEmail\": \"alice@example.com\"},\n        {\"id\": 2, \"oldName\": \"Bob\", \"currentEmail\": \"bob@example.com\"}\n    ]\n    \n    # Define the key changes you want to make\n    key_change_map = {\n        \"oldName\": \"full_name\",\n        \"currentEmail\": \"email\"\n    }\n    \n    # Rename the keys\n    transformed_data = rename_keys_in_list(sample_json_data, key_change_map)\n    \n    # Print the result\n    print(json.dumps(transformed_data, indent=2))\n```\n**Expected Output:**\n```json\n[\n  {\n    \"id\": 1,\n    \"full_name\": \"Alice\",\n    \"email\": \"alice@example.com\"\n  },\n  {\n    \"id\": 2,\n    \"full_name\": \"Bob\",\n    \"email\": \"bob@example.com\"\n  }\n]\n```\n\n#### Scenario 2: Renaming Files in a Directory\n\nThis script renames files in a folder based on a given mapping or pattern.\n\n```python\nimport os\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\ndef rename_files_in_directory(directory_path, name_mappings):\n    \"\"\"\n    Renames files in a specified directory based on a provided mapping.\n    \n    Args:\n        directory_path (str): Path to the directory containing the files.\n        name_mappings (dict): A dictionary where keys are current filenames and values are new filenames.\n    \"\"\"\n    path = Path(directory_path)\n    \n    for old_name, new_name in name_mappings.items():\n        old_file_path = path / old_name\n        new_file_path = path / new_name\n        \n        if old_file_path.exists():\n            old_file_path.rename(new_file_path)\n            print(f\"Renamed '{old_name}' to '{new_name}'\")\n        else:\n            print(f\"Warning: File '{old_name}' not found in directory.\")\n\n# Example usage\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    # Specify the folder containing the files to rename\n    target_directory = \"/path/to/your/files\"\n    \n    # Define the specific name changes\n    file_mappings = {\n        \"IMG_1234.jpg\": \"vacation_beach_sunset.jpg\",\n        \"report_Q3.pdf\": \"Quarterly_Financial_Report.pdf\",\n        \"old_script.py\": \"data_processing_final.py\"\n    }\n    \n    rename_files_in_directory(target_directory, file_mappings)\n```\n\n### 🤔 n8n vs. Python: How to Choose\n\nThe best approach depends on your goal. Here's a comparison to help you decide:\n\n| Feature | Using n8n's Rename Keys Node | Using a Custom Python Script |\n| :--- | :--- | :--- |\n| **Use Case** | **Inside an n8n workflow**, to reformat data between other nodes[citation:1]. | **Standalone task** or as part of a larger Python application. |\n| **Method** | Visual UI to map `Current Key Name` to `New Key Name`; can also use **Regex** for advanced pattern matching[citation:1]. | Writing code in a `.py` file. |\n| **Best For** | **Automations** involving multiple apps (e.g., receiving data from Google Sheets, renaming keys, then sending to a database). | **Scripting**, complex custom logic, or situations where a visual tool isn't needed. |\n\n### 🔍 How to Proceed\n\nTo get more specific help, you could:\n- **Clarify the context of \"keepitshot.com\"**, such as what kind of service it is or what specific data or files you want to rename.\n- **Define your goal**: Is this a one-time script, or part of a larger, ongoing automation?\n\nI hope this analysis and code provides a solid starting point.             "type": "RESPONSE",
            "content": "I found several effective methods to analyze and rename your images based on content. You can use AI vision analysis with OpenAI, traditional OCR for text recognition, or EXIF data extraction for organization by date.\n\nHere's a comparison of different approaches to help you choose:\n\n| **Method** | **Best For** | **Key Tools/Libraries** | **Pros & Cons** |\n| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |\n| **AI Vision Analysis** 🎯 | Understanding image content, objects, scenes, and context[citation:3][citation:5] | OpenAI API (`gpt-4o` or `gpt-4o-mini`)[citation:3][citation:5] | **Pros:** Deep understanding of content, very versatile<br>**Cons:** Requires API key and has associated costs |\n| **OCR (Text Recognition)** | Images containing visible text, screenshots, documents[citation:2][citation:4] | Tesseract OCR (`pytesseract`, `Pillow`)[citation:2][citation:4] | **Pros:** Free, good for specific text patterns<br>**Cons:** Only detects text, not image content |\n| **EXIF Data Extraction** | Photos from cameras/smartphones; organizing by date[citation:6] | `exifread` library[citation:6] | **Pros:** Free, uses existing metadata<br>**Cons:** Limited to metadata (date, camera), not content |\n\n### 🚀 Implementing the OpenAI API Method\n\nThis is the most powerful approach for understanding image content. Here is a Python script tailored to your request:\n\n```python\nimport os\nimport base64\nfrom openai import OpenAI\nimport re\n\ndef sanitize_filename(name):\n    \"\"\"Remove invalid characters from filenames.\"\"\"\n    return re.sub(r'[<>:\"/\\\\|?*]', \"\", name).strip()\n\ndef analyze_and_rename_images(folder_path, openai_api_key):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyzes images in a folder using OpenAI API and renames them based on content.\n    \n    Args:\n        folder_path (str): Path to the folder containing images\n        openai_api_key (str): Your OpenAI API key\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    # Initialize OpenAI client\n    client = OpenAI(api_key=openai_api_key)\n    \n    # Supported image formats\n    supported_formats = {'.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.gif', '.bmp', '.tiff', '.webp'}\n    \n    # Get list of image files\n    try:\n        image_files = [f for f in os.listdir(folder_path) \n                      if os.path.splitext(f)[1].lower() in supported_formats]\n    except FileNotFoundError:\n        print(f\"Error: Folder '{folder_path}' not found.\")\n        return\n    \n    if not image_files:\n        print(\"No image files found in the specified folder.\")\n        return\n    \n    print(f\"Found {len(image_files)} images to process...\")\n    \n    for filename in image_files:\n        file_path = os.path.join(folder_path, filename)\n        file_ext = os.path.splitext(filename)[1]\n        \n        try:\n            # Encode image to base64\n            with open(file_path, \"rb\") as image_file:\n                base64_image = base64.b64encode(image_file.read()).decode('utf-8')\n            \n            # Analyze image with OpenAI\n            response = client.chat.completions.create(\n                model=\"gpt-4o\",  # or \"gpt-4o-mini\" for cost efficiency\n                messages=[\n                    {\n                        \"role\": \"user\",\n                        \"content\": [\n                            {\n                                \"type\": \"text\", \n                                \"text\": \"Describe this image concisely in 5-7 words. Focus on the main subjects, style, colors, and any text if present. This description will be used as a filename, so make it descriptive but concise.\"\n                            },\n                            {\n                                \"type\": \"image_url\",\n                                \"image_url\": {\n                                    \"url\": f\"data:image/jpeg;base64,{base64_image}\"\n                                }\n                            }\n                        ]\n                    }\n                ],\n                max_tokens=150\n            )\n            \n            # Get the description from OpenAI\n            description = response.choices[0].message.content.strip()\n            safe_description = sanitize_filename(description)\n            \n            # Create new filename\n            new_filename = f\"{safe_description}{file_ext}\"\n            new_file_path = os.path.join(folder_path, new_filename)\n            \n            # Handle filename conflicts\n            counter = 1\n            while os.path.exists(new_file_path):\n                name_part, ext_part = os.path.splitext(new_filename)\n                new_filename = f\"{name_part}_{counter}{ext_part}\"\n                new_file_path = os.path.join(folder_path, new_filename)\n                counter += 1\n            \n            # Rename the file\n            os.rename(file_path, new_file_path)\n            print(f\"Renamed: '{filename}' -> '{new_filename}'\")\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"Error processing {filename}: {str(e)}\")\n    \n    print(\"Image renaming complete!\")\n\n# Usage for your specific case\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    # Set your folder path and API key\n    FOLDER_PATH = \"/Users/steven/Pictures/etsy\"\n    API_KEY = \"your_openai_api_key_here\"  # Replace with your actual API key\n    \n    # Run the function\n    analyze_and_rename_images(FOLDER_PATH, API_KEY)\n```\n\n**To use this script:**\n\n1. **Install required packages:**\n   ```bash\n   pip install openai\n   ```\n\n2. **Get an OpenAI API key** from [OpenAI's platform](https://platform.openai.com/)[citation:5]\n\n3. **Replace `\"your_openai_api_key_here\"`** with your actual API key in the script\n\n### 💡 Alternative Implementation Options\n\nIf the OpenAI method doesn't suit your needs, here are other approaches:\n\n**For OCR-based renaming (when images contain text):**\n```python\n# Basic structure using pytesseract[citation:2][citation:4]\nfrom PIL import Image\nimport pytesseract\nimport os\n\n# Configure tesseract path if needed\n# pytesseract.pytesseract.tesseract_cmd = r'/usr/bin/tesseract'\n\ndef rename_by_ocr(folder_path):\n    for filename in os.listdir(folder_path):\n        if filename.lower().endswith(('.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg')):\n            img_path = os.path.join(folder_path, filename)\n            image = Image.open(img_path)\n            text = pytesseract.image_to_string(image, lang='eng')\n            # Process extracted text for filename\n            # ... (clean and use text for new filename)\n```\n\n**For date-based organization:**\n```python\n# Using EXIF data[citation:6]\nimport exifread\nimport os\n\ndef rename_by_date(folder_path):\n    for filename in os.listdir(folder_path):\n        if filename.lower().endswith(('.jpg', '.jpeg')):\n            with open(os.path.join(folder_path, filename), 'rb') as f:\n                tags = exifread.process_file(f)\n                date_taken = str(tags.get('EXIF DateTimeOriginal', ''))\n                # Use date for filename organization\n```\n\n### 🔒 Important Considerations\n\n- **API Costs**: Be aware that using OpenAI's API incurs costs, though `gpt-4o-mini` is quite affordable for this use case[citation:5]\n- **Backup First**: Always backup your images before running batch renaming operations\n- **Rate Limiting**: The script includes basic error handling, but you may want to add delays between API calls if processing many images\n- **Filename Conflicts**: The script handles duplicate names by adding counters\n\nThe OpenAI approach will give you the most descriptive and useful filenames based on actual image content.             "type": "RESPONSE",
            "content": "I've found several powerful APIs you can use to create a script that analyzes and renames various file types based on their content. The best approach is to use a combination of specialized and multimodal AI services.\n\nHere is a comparison of the recommended APIs for your project:\n\n| **File Type** | **Recommended API** | **Key Analysis Capabilities** | **Renaming Strategy** |\n| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |\n| **Images** | **OpenAI GPT-4o**[citation:10] / **Google Vision AI**[citation:1][citation:5] | Object/scene detection, captioning, text extraction (OCR), landmark identification[citation:1][citation:5]. | Generate descriptive captions or use detected labels. |\n| **Documents (PDF)** | **Google Gemini API**[citation:6] / **Azure Document Intelligence**[citation:2] | Understands text, layout, images, tables, and diagrams; summarizes and extracts key information[citation:2][citation:6]. | Use document title, author, or summary of main topic. |\n| **Audio** | **Google Gemini API**[citation:7] | Transcription, content description, sentiment/topic analysis from speech[citation:7]. | Use transcript snippet, topic, or speaker information. |\n| **Video** | **Google Video Intelligence API**[citation:4][citation:8] | Object/action tracking, scene change detection, speech-to-text, label detection[citation:4][citation:8]. | Combine key scene labels and detected actions. |\n| **Code** | **General File Reading** | Read code structure, comments, and key functions (no specialized API needed). | Use project/function name and purpose from comments. |\n\n### 🛠️ How to Build Your File Analysis Script\n\nBelow is a Python script framework that integrates these APIs. You will need to install the required client libraries and set up API keys for the respective services.\n\n```python\nimport os\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\n# --- Configuration: Set your API keys here ---\nOPENAI_API_KEY = \"your_openai_api_key\"\nGOOGLE_API_KEY = \"your_google_api_key\" # For Gemini, Vision, Video AI\n\ndef sanitize_filename(name):\n    \"\"\"Remove characters that are invalid for filenames.\"\"\"\n    return re.sub(r'[<>:\"/\\\\|?*]', \"\", name).strip()\n\ndef analyze_and_rename_image(file_path):\n    \"\"\"Analyzes an image using OpenAI GPT-4o and renames it.\"\"\"\n    # Implementation example using OpenAI\n    from openai import OpenAI\n    client = OpenAI(api_key=OPENAI_API_KEY)\n    \n    # Read and encode the image\n    with open(file_path, \"rb\") as img_file:\n        image_data = img_file.read()\n    \n    response = client.chat.completions.create(\n        model=\"gpt-4o\",\n        messages=[\n            {\n                \"role\": \"user\",\n                \"content\": [\n                    {\"type\": \"text\", \"text\": \"Describe this image concisely in 5-7 words. Focus on the main subjects and scene.\"},\n                    {\"type\": \"image_url\", \"image_url\": {\"url\": f\"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_data}\"}}\n                ]\n            }\n        ],\n        max_tokens=150\n    )\n    description = response.choices[0].message.content.strip()\n    return sanitize_filename(description)\n\ndef analyze_and_rename_document(file_path):\n    \"\"\"Analyzes a PDF using Google Gemini API and renames it.\"\"\"\n    from google import genai\n    from google.genai import types\n    \n    client = genai.Client(api_key=GOOGLE_API_KEY)\n    \n    with open(file_path, \"rb\") as pdf_file:\n        pdf_data = pdf_file.read()\n    \n    response = client.models.generate_content(\n        model=\"gemini-2.5-flash\",\n        contents=[\n            types.Part.from_bytes(data=pdf_data, mime_type='application/pdf'),\n            \"What is the title or main topic of this document? Respond with a very short, concise phrase.\"\n        ]\n    )\n    topic = response.text.strip()\n    return sanitize_filename(topic)\n\ndef analyze_and_rename_audio(file_path):\n    \"\"\"Analyzes an audio file using Google Gemini API and renames it.\"\"\"\n    from google import genai\n    \n    client = genai.Client(api_key=GOOGLE_API_KEY)\n    \n    # Upload the file using the client\n    myfile = client.files.upload(file=file_path)\n    \n    response = client.models.generate_content(\n        model=\"gemini-2.5-flash\",\n        contents=[\"Summarize the main topic of this audio in a few words.\", myfile]\n    )\n    summary = response.text.strip()\n    return sanitize_filename(summary)\n\ndef analyze_and_rename_video(file_path):\n    \"\"\"Analyzes a video using Google Video Intelligence API and renames it.\"\"\"\n    # This is a conceptual example. Actual implementation requires Google Cloud Video Intelligence library.\n    # The API returns labels for scenes, objects, and actions.\n    # We'll use a placeholder function that returns a label string.\n    video_labels = \"video_analysis_placeholder\"\n    # In practice, you would use the Video Intelligence API to get prominent labels\n    # and concatenate them into a descriptive filename.\n    return sanitize_filename(video_labels)\n\ndef analyze_and_rename_code(file_path):\n    \"\"\"Reads a code file to determine its purpose for renaming.\"\"\"\n    try:\n        with open(file_path, \"r\", encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:\n            content = f.read()\n        \n        # Simple heuristic: look for a comment block at the top\n        lines = content.split('\\n')\n        description = \"\"\n        for line in lines[:10]:  # Check first 10 lines\n            if line.strip().startswith(('#', '//', '/*')):\n                clean_line = re.sub(r'^\\s*#\\s*|\\s*//\\s*|\\s*/\\*+\\s*|\\s*\\*+/', '', line).strip()\n                if clean_line and not clean_line.startswith('@'):\n                    description = clean_line\n                    break\n        \n        if not description:\n            # Fallback: use the name of the main function or class\n            func_match = re.search(r'(def|class)\\s+(\\w+)', content)\n            if func_match:\n                description = func_match.group(2)\n            else:\n                description = \"code_file\"\n        \n        return sanitize_filename(description)\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        return f\"code_file\"\n\ndef process_directory(directory_path):\n    \"\"\"Main function to process all files in a directory.\"\"\"\n    file_extensions = {\n        '.png': (analyze_and_rename_image, 'Image'),\n        '.jpg': (analyze_and_rename_image, 'Image'),\n        '.jpeg': (analyze_and_rename_image, 'Image'),\n        '.pdf': (analyze_and_rename_document, 'Document'),\n        '.mp3': (analyze_and_rename_audio, 'Audio'),\n        '.wav': (analyze_and_rename_audio, 'Audio'),\n        '.mp4': (analyze_and_rename_video, 'Video'),\n        '.avi': (analyze_and_rename_video, 'Video'),\n        '.py': (analyze_and_rename_code, 'Code'),\n        '.js': (analyze_and_rename_code, 'Code'),\n        '.java': (analyze_and_rename_code, 'Code'),\n    }\n    \n    for file_path in Path(directory_path).iterdir():\n        if file_path.is_file():\n            file_ext = file_path.suffix.lower()\n            if file_ext in file_extensions:\n                analyzer_func, file_type = file_extensions[file_ext]\n                print(f\"Processing {file_type} file: {file_path.name}\")\n                \n                try:\n                    new_name_base = analyzer_func(file_path)\n                    new_name = f\"{new_name_base}{file_ext}\"\n                    new_path = file_path.parent / new_name\n                    \n                    # Handle duplicate names\n                    counter = 1\n                    while new_path.exists():\n                        name_part, ext_part = os.path.splitext(new_name)\n                        new_name = f\"{name_part}_{counter}{ext_part}\"\n                        new_path = file_path.parent / new_name\n                        counter += 1\n                    \n                    file_path.rename(new_path)\n                    print(f\"Renamed to: {new_name}\")\n                    \n                except Exception as e:\n                    print(f\"Error processing {file_path.name}: {str(e)}\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    target_directory = \"/path/to/your/files\"  # Update this path\n    process_directory(target_directory)\n```\n\n### 💡 Implementation Notes and Best Practices\n\n- **API Keys and Costs**: You'll need to sign up for accounts with OpenAI and Google Cloud to get API keys. OpenAI client\n            if self.api_keys['openai']:\n                from openai import OpenAI\n                self.openai_client = OpenAI(api_key=self.api_keys['openai'])\n            else:\n                self.openai_client = None\n                logger.warning(\"OpenAI API key not found\")\n            \n            # Google client\n            if self.api_keys['google']:\n                from google import genai\n                self.google_client = genai.Client(api_key=self.api_keys['google'])\n            else:\n                self.google_client = None\n                logger.warning(\"Google API key not found\")\n                \n        except ImportError as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Missing required package: {e}\")\n            raise\n\n    def sanitize_filename(self, name: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Remove invalid characters from filenames\"\"\"\n        sanitized = re.sub(r'[<>:\"/\\\\|?*]', \"\", name)\n        sanitized = re.sub(r'\\s+', ' ', sanitized).strip()\n        return sanitized[:200]  # Limit length\n\n    def analyze_image_openai(self, file_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Analyze image using OpenAI GPT-4o\"\"\"\n        if not self.openai_client:\n            raise ValueError(\"OpenAI client not configured\")\n        \n        with open(file_path, \"rb\") as img_file:\n            image_data = base64.b64encode(img_file.read()).decode('utf-8')\n        \n        response = self.openai_client.chat.completions.create(\n            model=\"gpt-4o\",\n            messages=[\n                {\n                    \"role\": \"user\",\n                    \"content\": [\n                        {\n                            \"type\": \"text\",\n                            \"text\": \"Analyze this image and provide a concise, descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures the main subjects, scene, colors, and style. Focus on what would be most useful for file organization.\"\n                        },\n                        {\n                            \"type\": \"image_url\",\n                            \"image_url\": {\n                                \"url\": f\"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_data}\"\n                            }\n                        }\n                    ]\n                }\n            ],\n            max_tokens=150\n        )\n        return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()\n\n    def analyze_document_gemini(self, file_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Analyze document using Google Gemini\"\"\"\n        if not self.google_client:\n            raise ValueError(\"Google client not configured\")\n        \n        from google.genai import types\n        \n        mime_type = self.get_mime_type(file_path.suffix)\n        \n        with open(file_path, \"rb\") as file:\n            file_data = file.read()\n        \n        if file_path.suffix.lower() == '.pdf':\n            part = types.Part.from_bytes(data=file_data, mime_type=mime_type)\n        else:\n            # For text files, read as text\n            with open(file_path, \"r\", encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:\n                content = f.read(100000)  # Limit size\n            part = types.Part.from_text(text=content)\n        \n        response = self.google_client.models.generate_content(\n            model=\"gemini-2.0-flash\",\n            contents=[\n                part,\n                \"Analyze this document and provide a concise descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures the main topic, purpose, or content. Focus on what would be most useful for file organization.\"\n            ]\n        )\n        return response.text.strip()\n\n    def analyze_audio_gemini(self, file_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Analyze audio using Google Gemini\"\"\"\n        if not self.google_client:\n            raise ValueError(\"Google client not configured\")\n        \n        # Upload file to Google AI\n        uploaded_file = self.google_client.files.upload(file=file_path)\n        \n        response = self.google_client.models.generate_content(\n            model=\"gemini-2.0-flash\",\n            contents=[\n                \"Analyze this audio and provide a concise descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures the main content, topic, or purpose. Focus on what would be most useful for file organization.\",\n                uploaded_file\n            ]\n        )\n        return response.text.strip()\n\n    def analyze_video_gemini(self, file_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Analyze video using Google Gemini\"\"\"\n        if not self.google_client:\n            raise ValueError(\"Google client not configured\")\n        \n        uploaded_file = self.google_client.files.upload(file=file_path)\n        \n        response = self.google_client.models.generate_content(\n            model=\"gemini-2.0-flash\", \n            contents=[\n                \"Analyze this video and provide a concise descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures the main content, scene, or action. Focus on what would be most useful for file organization.\",\n                uploaded_file\n            ]\n        )\n        return response.text.strip()\n\n    def analyze_code_local(self, file_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Analyze code files using local file reading\"\"\"\n        try:\n            with open(file_path, \"r\", encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:\n                content = f.read(5000)  # Read first 5KB\n            \n            # Look for comments at the beginning of the file\n            lines = content.split('\\n')\n            description = \"\"\n            \n            for line in lines[:20]:  # Check first 20 lines\n                line = line.strip()\n                if line.startswith(('#', '//', '/*', '\"\"\"', \"'''\", '--')):\n                    # Clean the comment markers\n                    clean_line = re.sub(r'^\\s*#\\s*|\\s*//\\s*|\\s*/\\*+\\s*|\\s*\\*+/|\\s*\"\"\"\\s*|\\s*\\'\\'\\'\\s*', '', line)\n                    if clean_line and len(clean_line) > 5 and not clean_line.startswith('@'):\n                        description = clean_line\n                        break\n            \n            if not description:\n                # Look for function/class definitions\n                func_match = re.search(r'(def|class)\\s+(\\w+)', content)\n                if func_match:\n                    description = f\"{func_match.group(1)} {func_match.group(2)}\"\n                else:\n                    # Use file structure to guess purpose\n                    if 'import' in content and 'def ' in content:\n                        description = \"Python module with functions\"\n                    elif 'function' in content and '{' in content:\n                        description = \"JavaScript code with functions\"\n                    else:\n                        description = f\"Code file {file_path.stem}\"\n            \n            return description\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.warning(f\"Error analyzing code file {file_path}: {e}\")\n            return f\"code_file_{file_path.stem}\"\n\n    def get_mime_type(self, extension: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get MIME type from file extension\"\"\"\n        mime_map = {\n            '.pdf': 'application/pdf',\n            '.jpg': 'image/jpeg', \n            '.jpeg': 'image/jpeg',\n            '.png': 'image/png',\n            '.mp3': 'audio/mpeg',\n            '.wav': 'audio/wav',\n            '.mp4': 'video/mp4',\n            '.avi': 'video/x-msvideo',\n            '.mov': 'video/quicktime'\n        }\n        return mime_map.get(extension.lower(), 'application/octet-stream')\n\n    def analyze_file(self, file_path: Path) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Analyze file and return descriptive name\"\"\"\n        file_ext = file_path.suffix.lower()\n        \n        analysis_map = {\n            '.png': self.analyze_image_openai,\n            '.jpg': self.analyze_image_openai,\n            '.jpeg': self.analyze_image_openai,\n            '.pdf': self.analyze_document_gemini,\n            '.txt': self.analyze_document_gemini,\n            '.md': self.analyze_document_gemini,\n            '.mp3': self.analyze_audio_gemini,\n            '.wav': self.analyze_audio_gemini,\n            '.mp4': self.analyze_video_gemini,\n            '.avi': self.analyze_video_gemini,\n            '.mov': self.analyze_video_gemini,\n            '.py': self.analyze_code_local,\n            '.js': self.analyze_code_local,\n            '.java': self.analyze_code_local,\n            '.cpp': self.analyze_code_local,\n            '.html': self.analyze_code_local,\n            '.css': self.analyze_code_local\n        }\n        \n        if file_ext in analysis_map:\n            try:\n                analyzer_func = analysis_map[file_ext]\n                description = analyzer_func(file_path)\n                return self.sanitize_filename(description)\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.error(f\"Error analyzing {file_path}: {e}\")\n                return None\n        else:\n            logger.warning(f\"Unsupported file type: {file_ext}\")\n            return None\n\n    def rename_file(self, file_path: Path, new_name_base: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Rename file with conflict resolution\"\"\"\n        if not new_name_base:\n            return False\n        \n        new_filename = f\"{new_name_base}{file_path.suffix}\"\n        new_path = file_path.parent / new_filename\n        \n        # Handle duplicate names\n        counter = 1\n        while new_path.exists():\n            name_part, ext_part = os.path.splitext(new_filename)\n            new_filename = f\"{name_part}_{counter}{ext_part}\"\n            new_path = file_path.parent / new_filename\n            counter += 1\n        \n        try:\n            file_path.rename(new_path)\n            logger.info(f\"Renamed: '{file_path.name}' -> '{new_filename}'\")\n            return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Error renaming {file_path}: {e}\")\n            return False\n\n    def process_directory(self, directory_path: str, dry_run: bool = False):\n        \"\"\"Process all supported files in directory\"\"\"\n        target_path = Path(directory_path)\n        \n        if not target_path.exists():\n            logger.error(f\"Directory not found: {directory_path}\")\n            return\n        \n        supported_extensions = {'.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.pdf', '.txt', '.md', \n                              '.mp3', '.wav', '.mp4', '.avi', '.mov', \n                              '.py', '.js', '.java', '.cpp', '.html', '.css'}\n        \n        files_processed = 0\n        files_renamed = 0\n        \n        for file_path in target_path.iterdir():\n            if file_path.is_file() and file_path.suffix.lower() in supported_extensions:\n                files_processed += 1\n                logger.info(f\"Processing: {file_path.name}\")\n                \n                new_name = self.analyze_file(file_path)\n                if new_name:\n                    if dry_run:\n                        logger.info(f\"DRY RUN: Would rename '{file_path.name}' -> '{new_name}{file_path.suffix}'\")\n                    else:\n                        if self.rename_file(file_path, new_name):\n                            files_renamed += 1\n                else:\n                    logger.warning(f\"Could not generate name for: {file_path.name}\")\n        \n        logger.info(f\"Processing complete: {files_processed} files processed, {files_renamed} files renamed\")\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Main function with user interaction\"\"\"\n    import argparse\n    \n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description=\"AI-powered file analysis and renaming tool\")\n    parser.add_argument(\"directory\", help=\"Directory path to process\")\n    parser.add_argument(\"--dry-run\", action=\"store_true\", help=\"Show what would be renamed without actually doing it\")\n    parser.add_argument(\"--single-file\", help=\"Process a single file instead of directory\")\n    \n    args = parser.parse_args()\n    \n    analyzer = FileAnalyzer()\n    \n    if args.single_file:\n        file_path = Path(args.single_file)\n        if file_path.exists():\n            new_name = analyzer.analyze_file(file_path)\n            if new_name:\n                if args.dry_run:\n                    print(f\"DRY RUN: Would rename '{file_path.name}' -> '{new_name}{file_path.suffix}'\")\n                else:\n                    analyzer.rename_file(file_path, new_name)\n            else:\n                print(f\"Could not analyze {file_path.name}\")\n        else:\n            print(f\"File not found: {args.single_file}\")\n    else:\n        analyzer.process_directory(args.directory, args.dry_run)\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n```\n\n### 📋 Installation & Setup Requirements\n\n**Required Packages:**\n```bash\npip install openai google-genai python-dotenv\n```\n\n**Usage Examples:**\n```bash\n# Process entire directory\npython file_analyzer.py /Users/steven/Pictures/etsy\n\n# Dry run to see what would happen\npython file_analyzer.py /Users/steven/Pictures/etsy --dry-run\n\n# Process single file\npython file_analyzer.py --single-file /path/to/specific/file.jpg\n```\n\n## 🎯 AI Prompt to Replicate This System\n\nHere's the comprehensive prompt you can use with any capable AI to recreate The script is designed to be robust, user-friendly, and adaptable to your needs.\n\nHere is a complete solution that incorporates creative improvements and leverages the best tools for each file type.\n\n### 🤖 The Ultimate File Analysis & Renaming Script\n\nThe script below uses Google's Gemini API for its strong multi-format support (Images, Documents, Audio, Video) and includes a fallback mechanism for code files. It reads your API keys from a `~/.env` file as requested.\n\n```python\n#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nUltimate File Analyzer & Renamer\nEnhanced script with multi-API support, improved error handling, and better user feedback.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport re\nimport logging\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv\nimport base64\nfrom typing import Dict, Tuple, Callable, Optional\n\n# Load environment variables from home directory\nload_dotenv(Path.home() / '.env')\n\n# Configure logging\nlogging.basicConfig(\n    level=os.getenv('LOG_LEVEL', 'INFO'),\n    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'\n)\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\nclass UltimateFileAnalyzer:\n    \"\"\"Enhanced file analyzer with multi-API support and robust error handling\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.api_keys = {\n            'google': os.getenv('GOOGLE_API_KEY'),\n            'openai': os.getenv('OPENAI_API_KEY')\n        }\n        self.setup_clients()\n        self.processed_files = 0\n        self.skipped_files = 0\n        \n    def setup_clients(self):\n        \"\"\"Initialize API clients with fallback options\"\"\"\n        try:\n            # Google Gemini client (primary)\n            if self.api_keys['google']:\n                from google import genai\n                self.google_client = genai.Client(api_key=self.api_keys['google'])\n                logger.info(\"Google Gemini client initialized successfully\")\n            else:\n                self.google_client = None\n                logger.warning(\"Google API key not found\")\n                \n            # OpenAI client (fallback for images)\n            if self.api_keys['openai']:\n                from openai import OpenAI\n                self.openai_client = OpenAI(api_key=self.api_keys['openai'])\n                logger.info(\"OpenAI client initialized successfully\")\n            else:\n                self.openai_client = None\n                logger.warning(\"OpenAI API key not found\")\n                \n        except ImportError as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Missing required package: {e}\")\n            logger.info(\"Install required packages: pip install google-genai openai python-dotenv\")\n            raise\n\n    def sanitize_filename(self, name: str, max_length: int = 200) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Enhanced filename sanitization with length control\"\"\"\n        # Remove invalid characters and extra spaces\n        sanitized = re.sub(r'[<>:\"/\\\\|?*]', \"\", name)\n        sanitized = re.sub(r'\\s+', ' ', sanitized).strip()\n        \n        # Truncate to max length while preserving whole words if possible\n        if len(sanitized) > max_length:\n            truncated = sanitized[:max_length].rsplit(' ', 1)[0]\n            if len(truncated) > 0:\n                sanitized = truncated\n            else:\n                sanitized = sanitized[:max_length]\n                \n        return sanitized\n\n    def analyze_with_gemini(self, file_path: Path, prompt: str) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Unified Gemini analysis for multiple file types\"\"\"\n        if not self.google_client:\n            return None\n            \n        try:\n            # Upload and analyze file\n            uploaded_file = self.google_client.files.upload(file=file_path)\n            response = self.google_client.models.generate_content(\n                model=\"gemini-1.5-flash\",\n                contents=[prompt, uploaded_file]\n            )\n            return response.text.strip()\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Gemini analysis failed for {file_path.name}: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def analyze_image_fallback(self, file_path: Path) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Fallback image analysis using OpenAI\"\"\"\n        if not self.openai_client:\n            return None\n            \n        try:\n            with open(file_path, \"rb\") as img_file:\n                image_data = base64.b64encode(img_file.read()).decode('utf-8')\n            \n            response = self.openai_client.chat.completions.create(\n                model=\"gpt-4o\",\n                messages=[\n                    {\n                        \"role\": \"user\",\n                        \"content\": [\n                            {\n                                \"type\": \"text\",\n                                \"text\": \"Analyze this image and provide a concise, descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures the main subjects, scene, colors, and style. Focus on what would be most useful for file organization.\"\n                            },\n                            {\n                                \"type\": \"image_url\",\n                                \"image_url\": {\n                                    \"url\": f\"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_data}\"\n                                }\n                            }\n                        ]\n                    }\n                ],\n                max_tokens=150\n            )\n            return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"OpenAI image analysis failed: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def analyze_code_intelligently(self, file_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Enhanced code file analysis with structure detection\"\"\"\n        try:\n            with open(file_path, \"r\", encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:\n                content = f.read(10000)  # Increased limit for better analysis\n            \n            # Enhanced comment detection\n            lines = content.split('\\n')\n            description = \"\"\n            \n            # Look for structured comments (docstrings, header comments)\n            comment_indicators = [\n                ('\"\"\"', '\"\"\"'), (\"'''\", \"'''\"),  # Python docstrings\n                ('/*', '*/'),  # Multi-line comments\n                ('#', ''), ('//', '')  # Single-line comments\n            ]\n            \n            for start, end in comment_indicators:\n                if start in content[:1000]:  # Check first 1000 chars\n                    if end:\n                        pattern = re.escape(start) + r'(.*?)' + re.escape(end)\n                        match = re.search(pattern, content, re.DOTALL)\n                        if match:\n                            candidate = match.group(1).strip()\n                            # Take first meaningful line\n                            first_line = candidate.split('\\n')[0].strip()\n                            if len(first_line) > 10 and not first_line.startswith(('@', 'TODO')):\n                                description = first_line\n                                break\n                    else:\n                        # Single-line comments\n                        for line in lines[:20]:\n                            if line.strip().startswith(start):\n                                clean_line = line.strip()[len(start):].strip()\n                                if clean_line and len(clean_line) > 5:\n                                    description = clean_line\n                                    break\n            \n            # Fallback to code structure analysis\n            if not description:\n                # Detect main components\n                if 'def ' in content and 'class ' in content:\n                    func_match = re.search(r'def\\s+(\\w+)', content)\n                    class_match = re.search(r'class\\s+(\\w+)', content)\n                    if func_match and class_match:\n                        description = f\"{class_match.group(1)} class with {func_match.group(1)} method\"\n                elif 'function ' in content:\n                    func_match = re.search(r'function\\s+(\\w+)', content)\n                    description = f\"JavaScript {func_match.group(1) if func_match else 'function'}\"\n                elif 'def ' in content:\n                    func_match = re.search(r'def\\s+(\\w+)', content)\n                    description = f\"Python {func_match.group(1) if func_match else 'function'}\"\n                elif 'class ' in content:\n                    class_match = re.search(r'class\\s+(\\w+)', content)\n                    description = f\"Python {class_match.group(1) if class_match else 'class'}\"\n                else:\n                    # Analyze file purpose based on content\n                    if 'import' in content and 'def ' in content:\n                        description = \"Python module with functions\"\n                    elif 'require' in content or 'import' in content:\n                        description = \"JavaScript module\"\n                    elif '<html' in content.lower() or '<div' in content.lower():\n                        description = \"HTML document\"\n                    elif '.container' in content or 'margin:' in content:\n                        description = \"CSS stylesheet\"\n                    else:\n                        description = f\"{file_path.stem} code file\"\n            \n            return description\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.warning(f\"Code analysis failed for {file_path}: {e}\")\n            return f\"code_file_{file_path.stem}\"\n\n    def get_file_analysis_prompt(self, file_type: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get optimized prompts for different file types\"\"\"\n        prompts = {\n            'image': \"Analyze this image and provide a concise, descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures the main subjects, scene, colors, and style. Focus on what would be most useful for file organization.\",\n            'document': \"Analyze this document and provide a concise descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures the main topic, purpose, or content. Focus on what would be most useful for file organization.\",\n            'audio': \"Analyze this audio file and provide a concise descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures the main content, topic, or purpose. Focus on what would be most useful for file organization.\",\n            'video': \"Analyze this video and provide a concise descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures the main content, scene, or action. Focus on what would be most useful for file organization.\"\n        }\n        return prompts.get(file_type, prompts['document'])\n\n    def analyze_file(self, file_path: Path) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Enhanced file analysis with multiple fallback strategies\"\"\"\n        file_ext = file_path.suffix.lower()\n        \n        # File type categorization\n        file_categories = {\n            'image': ['.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.gif', '.bmp', '.tiff', '.webp'],\n            'document': ['.pdf', '.txt', '.md', '.docx', '.pptx'],\n            'audio': ['.mp3', '.wav', '.m4a', '.flac', '.aac'],\n            'video': ['.mp4', '.avi', '.mov', '.mkv', '.wmv'],\n            'code': ['.py', '.js', '.java', '.cpp', '.c', '.html', '.css', '.php', '.rb', '.go']\n        }\n        \n        # Determine file category\n        file_category = 'document'  # default\n        for category, extensions in file_categories.items():\n            if file_ext in extensions:\n                file_category = category\n                break\n        \n        try:\n            # Use Gemini for supported types\n            if file_category in ['image', 'document', 'audio', 'video']:\n                prompt = self.get_file_analysis_prompt(file_category)\n                description = self.analyze_with_gemini(file_path, prompt)\n                \n                # Fallback for images using OpenAI\n                if not description and file_category == 'image':\n                    description = self.analyze_image_fallback(file_path)\n                    \n            elif file_category == 'code':\n                description = self.analyze_code_intelligently(file_path)\n            else:\n                logger.warning(f\"Unsupported file category for {file_path.name}\")\n                return None\n            \n            if description:\n                return self.sanitize_filename(description)\n            else:\n                logger.warning(f\"Could not generate description for {file_path.name}\")\n                return None\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Analysis failed for {file_path.name}: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def rename_file(self, file_path: Path, new_name_base: str, dry_run: bool = False) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Enhanced file renaming with conflict resolution and dry run support\"\"\"\n        if not new_name_base:\n            return False\n        \n        new_filename = f\"{new_name_base}{file_path.suffix}\"\n        new_path = file_path.parent / new_filename\n        \n        # Handle duplicate names with smart numbering\n        counter = 1\n        while new_path.exists():\n            name_part, ext_part = os.path.splitext(new_filename)\n            # Remove existing counter if present\n            name_part = re.sub(r'_\\d+$', '', name_part)\n            new_filename = f\"{name_part}_{counter}{ext_part}\"\n            new_path = file_path.parent / new_filename\n            counter += 1\n        \n        try:\n            if not dry_run:\n                file_path.rename(new_path)\n                logger.info(f\"✅ Renamed: '{file_path.name}' -> '{new_filename}'\")\n            else:\n                logger.info(f\"🔍 DRY RUN: Would rename '{file_path.name}' -> '{new_filename}'\")\n            return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"❌ Error renaming {file_path.name}: {e}\")\n            return False\n\n    def process_directory(self, directory_path: str, dry_run: bool = False):\n        \"\"\"Enhanced directory processing with progress tracking\"\"\"\n        target_path = Path(directory_path)\n        \n        if not target_path.exists():\n            logger.error(f\"❌ Directory not found: {directory_path}\")\n            return\n        \n        # Supported file extensions\n        supported_extensions = {\n            '.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.gif', '.bmp', '.tiff', '.webp',  # Images\n            '.pdf', '.txt', '.md', '.docx', '.pptx',  # Documents\n            '.mp3', '.wav', '.m4a', '.flac', '.aac',  # Audio\n            '.mp4', '.avi', '.mov', '.mkv', '.wmv',   # Video\n            '.py', '.js', '.java', '.cpp', '.c', '.html', '.css', '.php', '.rb', '.go'  # Code\n        }\n        \n        files_processed = 0\n        files_renamed = 0\n        \n        logger.info(f\"🎯 Starting processing of: {directory_path}\")\n        if dry_run:\n            logger.info(\"🔍 DRY RUN MODE - No files will be modified\")\n        \n        # Get all supported files\n        file_list = []\n        for file_path in target_path.iterdir():\n            if file_path.is_file() and file_path.suffix.lower() in supported_extensions:\n                file_list.append(file_path)\n        \n        total_files = len(file_list)\n        logger.info(f\"📁 Found {total_files} supported files to process\")\n        \n        for file_path in file_list:\n            files_processed += 1\n            logger.info(f\"🔍 Analyzing ({files_processed}/{total_files}): {file_path.name}\")\n            \n            new_name = self.analyze_file(file_path)\n            if new_name:\n                if self.rename_file(file_path, new_name, dry_run):\n                    if not dry_run:\n                        files_renamed += 1\n            else:\n                self.skipped_files += 1\n                logger.warning(f\"⏭️  Skipped: {file_path.name}\")\n        \n        # Summary report\n        logger.info(\"=\" * 50)\n        logger.info(\"📊 PROCESSING SUMMARY\")\n        logger.info(f\"📁 Directory: {directory_path}\")\n        logger.info(f\"📄 Files processed: {files_processed}\")\n        if dry_run:\n            logger.info(f\"🔍 Files that would be renamed: {files_processed - self.skipped_files}\")\n            logger.info(\"💡 This was a dry run. No files were modified.\")\n        else:\n            logger.info(f\"✅ Files successfully renamed: {files_renamed}\")\n            logger.info(f\"⏭️  Files skipped: {self.skipped_files}\")\n        logger.info(\"=\" * 50)\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Enhanced main function with argument parsing\"\"\"\n    import argparse\n    \n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description=\"🎯 Ultimate File Analyzer & Renamer - AI-powered file organization\",\n        formatter_class=argparse.RawDescriptionHelpFormatter,\n        epilog=\"\"\"\nExamples:\n  # Process a directory\n  python file_analyzer.py /Users/steven/Pictures/etsy\n  \n  # Dry run to see what would happen\n  python file_analyzer.py /path/to/files --dry-run\n  \n  # Process single file\n  python file_analyzer.py --single-file /path/to/image.jpg\n        \"\"\"\n    )\n    \n    parser.add_argument(\"directory\", nargs=\"?\", help=\"Directory path to process\")\n    parser.add_argument(\"--dry-run\", action=\"store_true\", help=\"Show what would be renamed without actually doing it\")\n    parser.add_argument(\"--single-file\", help=\"Process a single file instead of directory\")\n    parser.add_argument(\"--verbose\", action=\"store_true\", help=\"Enable verbose logging\")\n    \n    args = parser.parse_args()\n    \n    if args.verbose:\n        logging.getLogger().setLevel(logging.DEBUG)\n    \n    if not args.directory and not args.single_file:\n        parser.print_help()\n        return\n    \n    analyzer = UltimateFileAnalyzer()\n    \n    try:\n        if args.single_file:\n            file_path = Path(args.single_file)\n            if file_path.exists():\n                new_name = analyzer.analyze_file(file_path)\n                if new_name:\n                    analyzer.rename_file(file_path, new_name, args.dry_run)\n                else:\n                    logger.error(f\"❌ Could not analyze {file_path.name}\")\n            else:\n                logger.error(f\"❌ File not found: {args.single_file}\")\n        else:\n            analyzer.process_directory(args.directory, args.dry_run)\n    except KeyboardInterrupt:\n        logger.info(\"🛑 Operation cancelled by user\")\n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f\"💥 Unexpected error: {e}\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n```\n\n### 🚀 Creative Document Organizer Script\n\n**`organize_documents.sh`**\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n\n# Document Analysis & Organization Script\n# Specialized for PDF, DOCX, TXT, MD, PPTX files\n\nset -e\n\n# Colors\nRED='\\033[0;31m'\nGREEN='\\033[0;32m'\nYELLOW='\\033[1;33m'\nBLUE='\\033[0;34m'\nNC='\\033[0m'\n\nlog_info() { echo -e \"${BLUE}[DOCS]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_success() { echo -e \"${GREEN}[SUCCESS]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_warning() { echo -e \"${YELLOW}[WARNING]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_error() { echo -e \"${RED}[ERROR]${NC} $1\"; }\n\nload_env() {\n    if [ -f ~/.env ]; then\n        source ~/.env\n        log_info \"Environment loaded\"\n    else\n        log_error \"~/.env file not found\"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n}\n\ninstall_document_deps() {\n    log_info \"Installing document processing dependencies...\"\n    \n    # Install Python packages for document processing\n    pip install google-genai python-dotenv PyPDF2 python-docx pdfplumber\n    \n    log_success \"Document dependencies installed\"\n}\n\nanalyze_document_with_gemini() {\n    local file_path=\"$1\"\n    local mime_type=\"$2\"\n    \n    if [ -z \"$GOOGLE_API_KEY\" ]; then\n        log_error \"GOOGLE_API_KEY not set\"\n        return 1\n    fi\n    \n    # Use python for document analysis\n    python3 - << EOF\nimport os\nimport sys\nfrom google import genai\nfrom google.genai import types\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\ndef analyze_document(file_path, mime_type):\n    try:\n        client = genai.Client(api_key=os.getenv('GOOGLE_API_KEY'))\n        \n        with open(file_path, 'rb') as f:\n            file_data = f.read()\n        \n        if mime_type == 'application/pdf':\n            part = types.Part.from_bytes(data=file_data, mime_type=mime_type)\n        else:\n            # For text-based documents, read as text\n            try:\n                with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as txt_file:\n                    content = txt_file.read(50000)  # Limit size\n                part = types.Part.from_text(text=content)\n            except:\n                part = types.Part.from_bytes(data=file_data, mime_type=mime_type)\n        \n        response = client.models.generate_content(\n            model=\"gemini-1.5-flash\",\n            contents=[\n                part,\n                \"Analyze this document and provide a concise descriptive filename (4-6 words) that captures: document type, main topic, purpose, author if visible, and key subjects. Focus on creating a useful filename for organization.\"\n            ]\n        )\n        return response.text.strip()\n    except Exception as e:\n        return f\"document_analysis_error\"\n\nresult = analyze_document(\"$file_path\", \"$mime_type\")\nprint(result)\nEOF\n}\n\nget_document_mime_type() {\n    local file=\"$1\"\n    case \"${file##*.}\" in\n        pdf) echo \"application/pdf\" ;;\n        docx) echo \"application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document\" ;;\n        txt) echo \"text/plain\" ;;\n        md) echo \"text/markdown\" ;;\n        pptx) echo \"application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.presentationml.presentation\" ;;\n        *) echo \"application/octet-stream\" ;;\n    esac\n}\n\nsanitize_filename() {\n    echo \"$1\" | sed 's/[<>:\"/\\\\|?*]//g' | sed 's/^[[:space:]]*//;s/[[:space:]]*$//' | cut -c1-150\n}\n\norganize_documents() {\n    local target_dir=\"${1:-.}\"\n    local dry_run=\"${2:-false}\"\n    \n    log_info \"Starting document organization in: $target_dir\"\n    \n    # Supported document formats\n    document_extensions=(\"pdf\" \"docx\" \"txt\" \"md\" \"pptx\" \"doc\" \"odt\" \"rtf\")\n    \n    find \"$target_dir\" -type f \\( \\\n        -iname \"*.pdf\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.docx\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.txt\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.md\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.pptx\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.doc\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.odt\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.rtf\" \\\n    \\) | while read -r file; do\n        filename=$(basename \"$file\")\n        extension=\"${filename##*.}\"\n        base_name=$(basename \"$file\" \".$extension\")\n        \n        log_info \"Processing: $filename\"\n        \n        mime_type=$(get_document_mime_type \"$file\")\n        new_name=$(analyze_document_with_gemini \"$file\" \"$mime_type\")\n        \n        if [ $? -eq 0 ] && [ -n \"$new_name\" ] && [ \"$new_name\" != \"document_analysis_error\" ]; then\n            sanitized_name=$(sanitize_filename \"$new_name\")\n            new_filename=\"${sanitized_name}.${extension}\"\n            new_path=$(dirname \"$file\")/\"$new_filename\"\n            \n            # Handle duplicates\n            counter=1\n            while [ -f \"$new_path\" ]; do\n                name_part=\"${sanitized_name}\"\n                new_filename=\"${name_part}_${counter}.${extension}\"\n                new_path=$(dirname \"$file\")/\"$new_filename\"\n                counter=$((counter + 1))\n            done\n            \n            if [ \"$dry_run\" = \"true\" ]; then\n                log_info \"DRY RUN: Would rename '$filename' -> '$new_filename'\"\n            else\n                mv \"$file\" \"$new_path\"\n                log_success \"Renamed: $filename -> $new_filename\"\n            fi\n        else\n            log_warning \"Could not analyze document: $filename\"\n        fi\n    done\n    \n    log_success \"Document organization completed\"\n}\n\nmain() {\n    load_env\n    \n    local target_dir=\"${1:-.}\"\n    local dry_run=\"${2:-false}\"\n    \n    case \"$dry_run\" in\n        true|1|yes) dry_run=\"true\" ;;\n        *) dry_run=\"false\" ;;\n    esac\n    \n    organize_documents \"$target_dir\" \"$dry_run\"\n}\n\n# If script is executed directly\nif [[ \"${BASH_SOURCE[0]}\" == \"${0}\" ]]; then\n    main \"$@\"\nfi\n```\n\n## 🎵 2. Audio/Video Organizer Script\n\n**`organize_audio_video.sh`**\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n\n# Audio/Video Analysis & Organization Script\n# Specialized for MP3, MP4, WAV, AVI, MOV files\n\nset -e\n\n# Colors\nRED='\\033[0;31m'\nGREEN='\\033[0;32m'\nYELLOW='\\033[1;33m'\nBLUE='\\033[0;34m'\nPURPLE='\\033[0;35m'\nNC='\\033[0m'\n\nlog_info() { echo -e \"${PURPLE}[AUDIO/VIDEO]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_success() { echo -e \"${GREEN}[SUCCESS]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_warning() { echo -e \"${YELLOW}[WARNING]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_error() { echo -e \"${RED}[ERROR]${NC} $1\"; }\n\nload_env() {\n    if [ -f ~/.env ]; then\n        source ~/.env\n        log_info \"Environment loaded\"\n    else\n        log_error \"~/.env file not found\"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n}\n\ninstall_av_deps() {\n    log_info \"Installing audio/video processing dependencies...\"\n    \n    # Install required tools\n    pip install google-genai python-dotenv mutagen\n    \n    # Install ffmpeg for media analysis (on macOS)\n    if ! command -v ffmpeg &> /dev/null; then\n        log_info \"Installing ffmpeg...\"\n        brew install ffmpeg\n    fi\n    \n    log_success \"Audio/Video dependencies installed\"\n}\n\nanalyze_media_with_gemini() {\n    local file_path=\"$1\"\n    local media_type=\"$2\"  # \"audio\" or \"video\"\n    \n    if [ -z \"$GOOGLE_API_KEY\" ]; then\n        log_error \"GOOGLE_API_KEY not set\"\n        return 1\n    fi\n    \n    python3 - << EOF\nimport os\nimport sys\nfrom google import genai\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\ndef analyze_media(file_path, media_type):\n    try:\n        client = genai.Client(api_key=os.getenv('GOOGLE_API_KEY'))\n        \n        # Upload file to Google AI\n        uploaded_file = client.files.upload(file=file_path)\n        \n        if media_type == \"audio\":\n            prompt = \"Analyze this audio file and provide a concise descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures: content type (music, podcast, recording), main topic or title, mood/tone, speaker/artist if identifiable, and key themes.\"\n        else:\n            prompt = \"Analyze this video and provide a concise descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures: video type, main subject/scene, key actions, setting/location, and primary content focus.\"\n        \n        response = client.models.generate_content(\n            model=\"gemini-1.5-flash\",\n            contents=[prompt, uploaded_file]\n        )\n        return response.text.strip()\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"media_analysis_error: {str(e)}\")\n        return \"media_analysis_error\"\n\nresult = analyze_media(\"$file_path\", \"$media_type\")\nprint(result)\nEOF\n}\n\nextract_media_metadata() {\n    local file=\"$1\"\n    local media_type=\"$2\"\n    \n    python3 - << EOF\nimport os\nimport sys\nfrom mutagen import File\nfrom mutagen.easyid3 import EasyID3\nfrom datetime import datetime\nimport subprocess\n\ndef extract_metadata(file_path, media_type):\n    try:\n        metadata = {}\n        \n        if media_type == \"audio\":\n            # Try to extract ID3 tags for audio\n            try:\n                audio = EasyID3(file_path)\n                if audio:\n                    metadata['title'] = audio.get('title', [None])[0]\n                    metadata['artist'] = audio.get('artist', [None])[0]\n                    metadata['album'] = audio.get('album', [None])[0]\n            except:\n                pass\n            \n            # Try to get duration using ffmpeg\n            try:\n                result = subprocess.run([\n                    'ffprobe', '-v', 'quiet', '-show_entries', 'format=duration',\n                    '-of', 'csv=p=0', file_path\n                ], capture_output=True, text=True)\n                duration = float(result.stdout.strip())\n                mins = int(duration // 60)\n                secs = int(duration % 60)\n                metadata['duration'] = f\"{mins}m{secs}s\"\n            except:\n                metadata['duration'] = None\n                \n        elif media_type == \"video\":\n            # Extract video metadata\n            try:\n                result = subprocess.run([\n                    'ffprobe', '-v', 'quiet', '-show_entries', 'stream=codec_type:format=duration',\n                    '-of', 'csv=p=0', file_path\n                ], capture_output=True, text=True)\n                lines = result.stdout.strip().split('\\n')\n                metadata['has_video'] = any('video' in line for line in lines)\n                metadata['has_audio'] = any('audio' in line for line in lines)\n                \n                # Get duration\n                duration_line = [line for line in lines if line and not ('video' in line or 'audio' in line)]\n                if duration_line:\n                    duration = float(duration_line[0])\n                    mins = int(duration // 60)\n                    secs = int(duration % 60)\n                    metadata['duration'] = f\"{mins}m{secs}s\"\n            except:\n                metadata['duration'] = None\n        \n        # File stats\n        stat = os.stat(file_path)\n        metadata['size_mb'] = round(stat.st_size / (1024 * 1024), 2)\n        metadata['modified'] = datetime.fromtimestamp(stat.st_mtime).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n        \n        return metadata\n    except Exception as e:\n        return {\"error\": str(e)}\n\nmetadata = extract_metadata(\"$file\", \"$media_type\")\nfor key, value in metadata.items():\n    print(f\"{key}={value}\")\nEOF\n}\n\nget_media_type() {\n    local file=\"$1\"\n    case \"${file##*.}\" in\n        mp3|wav|m4a|flac|aac|ogg) echo \"audio\" ;;\n        mp4|avi|mov|mkv|wmv|flv|m4v) echo \"video\" ;;\n        *) echo \"unknown\" ;;\n    esac\n}\n\nsanitize_filename() {\n    echo \"$1\" | sed 's/[<>:\"/\\\\|?*]//g' | sed 's/^[[:space:]]*//;s/[[:space:]]*$//' | cut -c1-150\n}\n\norganize_media() {\n    local target_dir=\"${1:-.}\"\n    local dry_run=\"${2:-false}\"\n    \n    log_info \"Starting media organization in: $target_dir\"\n    \n    # Find all media files\n    find \"$target_dir\" -type f \\( \\\n        -iname \"*.mp3\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.wav\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.m4a\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.flac\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.aac\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.ogg\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.mp4\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.avi\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.mov\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.mkv\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.wmv\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.flv\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.m4v\" \\\n    \\) | while read -r file; do\n        filename=$(basename \"$file\")\n        extension=\"${filename##*.}\"\n        media_type=$(get_media_type \"$file\")\n        \n        log_info \"Processing $media_type: $filename\"\n        \n        # Extract basic metadata first\n        log_info \"Extracting metadata...\"\n        while IFS='=' read -r key value; do\n            case \"$key\" in\n                title) title=\"$value\" ;;\n                artist) artist=\"$value\" ;;\n                duration) duration=\"$value\" ;;\n                size_mb) size_mb=\"$value\" ;;\n            esac\n        done < <(extract_media_metadata \"$file\" \"$media_type\")\n        \n        # Use AI analysis\n        new_name=$(analyze_media_with_gemini \"$file\" \"$media_type\")\n        \n        if [ $? -eq 0 ] && [ -n \"$new_name\" ] && [ \"$new_name\" != \"media_analysis_error\" ]; then\n            sanitized_name=$(sanitize_filename \"$new_name\")\n            new_filename=\"${sanitized_name}.${extension}\"\n            new_path=$(dirname \"$file\")/\"$new_filename\"\n            \n            # Handle duplicates\n            counter=1\n            while [ -f \"$new_path\" ]; do\n                name_part=\"${sanitized_name}\"\n                new_filename=\"${name_part}_${counter}.${extension}\"\n                new_path=$(dirname \"$file\")/\"$new_filename\"\n                counter=$((counter + 1))\n            done\n            \n            if [ \"$dry_run\" = \"true\" ]; then\n                log_info \"DRY RUN: Would rename '$filename' -> '$new_filename'\"\n                if [ -n \"$duration\" ]; then\n                    log_info \"Metadata: Duration=${duration}, Size=${size_mb}MB\"\n                fi\n            else\n                mv \"$file\" \"$new_path\"\n                log_success \"Renamed: $filename -> $new_filename\"\n            fi\n        else\n            # Fallback to metadata-based naming\n            if [ -n \"$title\" ] && [ \"$title\" != \"None\" ]; then\n                fallback_name=\"$title\"\n                if [ -n \"$artist\" ] && [ \"$artist\" != \"None\" ]; then\n                    fallback_name=\"${artist} - ${title}\"\n                fi\n            else\n                fallback_name=\"${media_type}_file_${filename%.*}\"\n            fi\n            \n            sanitized_name=$(sanitize_filename \"$fallback_name\")\n            new_filename=\"${sanitized_name}.${extension}\"\n            new_path=$(dirname \"$file\")/\"$new_filename\"\n            \n            if [ \"$dry_run\" = \"true\" ]; then\n                log_info \"DRY RUN: Would rename '$filename' -> '$new_filename' (metadata fallback)\"\n            else\n                mv \"$file\" \"$new_path\"\n                log_success \"Renamed using metadata: $filename -> $new_filename\"\n            fi\n        fi\n    done\n    \n    log_success \"Media organization completed\"\n}\n\nmain() {\n    load_env\n    \n    local target_dir=\"${1:-.}\"\n    local dry_run=\"${2:-false}\"\n    \n    case \"$dry_run\" in\n        true|1|yes) dry_run=\"true\" ;;\n        *) dry_run=\"false\" ;;\n    esac\n    \n    organize_media \"$target_dir\" \"$dry_run\"\n}\n\nif [[ \"${BASH_SOURCE[0]}\" == \"${0}\" ]]; then\n    main \"$@\"\nfi\n```\n\n## 🖼️ 3. Image Organizer Script\n\n**`organize_images.sh`**\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n\n# Image Analysis & Organization Script\n# Specialized for PNG, JPG, JPEG, GIF, WebP, TIFF files\n\nset -e\n\n# Colors\nRED='\\033[0;31m'\nGREEN='\\033[0;32m'\nYELLOW='\\033[1;33m'\nBLUE='\\033[0;34m'\nCYAN='\\033[0;36m'\nNC='\\033[0m'\n\nlog_info() { echo -e \"${CYAN}[IMAGES]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_success() { echo -e \"${GREEN}[SUCCESS]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_warning() { echo -e \"${YELLOW}[WARNING]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_error() { echo -e \"${RED}[ERROR]${NC} $1\"; }\n\nload_env() {\n    if [ -f ~/.env ]; then\n        source ~/.env\n        log_info \"Environment loaded\"\n    else\n        log_error \"~/.env file not found\"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n}\n\ninstall_image_deps() {\n    log_info \"Installing image processing dependencies...\"\n    \n    # Install Python packages\n    pip install google-genai openai python-dotenv Pillow\n    \n    # Install image tools on macOS\n    if ! command -v identify &> /dev/null; then\n        log_info \"Installing ImageMagick for image analysis...\"\n        brew install imagemagick\n    fi\n    \n    log_success \"Image dependencies installed\"\n}\n\nanalyze_image_with_gemini() {\n    local file_path=\"$1\"\n    \n    if [ -z \"$GOOGLE_API_KEY\" ]; then\n        log_error \"GOOGLE_API_KEY not set\"\n        return 1\n    fi\n    \n    python3 - << EOF\nimport os\nimport base64\nfrom google import genai\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\ndef analyze_image(file_path):\n    try:\n        client = genai.Client(api_key=os.getenv('GOOGLE_API_KEY'))\n        \n        # Upload image to Google AI\n        uploaded_file = client.files.upload(file=file_path)\n        \n        response = client.models.generate_content(\n            model=\"gemini-1.5-flash\",\n            contents=[\n                \"Analyze this image and provide a concise descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures: main subjects/objects, scene/setting, colors/mood, style/type (photo, art, diagram), composition, and any notable features. Focus on creating searchable, organized filenames.\",\n                uploaded_file\n            ]\n        )\n        return response.text.strip()\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"image_analysis_error: {str(e)}\")\n        return \"image_analysis_error\"\n\nresult = analyze_image(\"$file_path\")\nprint(result)\nEOF\n}\n\nanalyze_image_with_openai() {\n    local file_path=\"$1\"\n    \n    if [ -z \"$OPENAI_API_KEY\" ]; then\n        log_error \"OPENAI_API_KEY not set\"\n        return 1\n    fi\n    \n    python3 - << EOF\nimport os\nimport base64\nfrom openai import OpenAI\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\ndef analyze_image_openai(file_path):\n    try:\n        client = OpenAI(api_key=os.getenv('OPENAI_API_KEY'))\n        \n        with open(file_path, \"rb\") as img_file:\n            image_data = base64.b64encode(img_file.read()).decode('utf-8')\n        \n        response = client.chat.completions.create(\n            model=\"gpt-4o\",\n            messages=[\n                {\n                    \"role\": \"user\",\n                    \"content\": [\n                        {\n                            \"type\": \"text\",\n                            \"text\": \"Analyze this image and provide a concise descriptive filename (5-7 words) that captures the main subjects, scene, colors, style, composition, and mood. Focus on creating organized, searchable filenames.\"\n                        },\n                        {\n                            \"type\": \"image_url\",\n                            \"image_url\": {\n                                \"url\": f\"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_data}\"\n                            }\n                        }\n                    ]\n                }\n            ],\n            max_tokens=150\n        )\n        return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"openai_analysis_error: {str(e)}\")\n        return \"openai_analysis_error\"\n\nresult = analyze_image_openai(\"$file_path\")\nprint(result)\nEOF\n}\n\nextract_image_metadata() {\n    local file=\"$1\"\n    \n    python3 - << EOF\nimport os\nfrom PIL import Image\nfrom PIL.ExifTags import TAGS\nfrom datetime import datetime\nimport subprocess\n\ndef extract_image_metadata(file_path):\n    try:\n        metadata = {}\n        \n        with Image.open(file_path) as img:\n            # Basic image info\n            metadata['format'] = img.format\n            metadata['mode'] = img.mode\n            metadata['size'] = f\"{img.width}x{img.height}\"\n            metadata['megapixels'] = round((img.width * img.height) / 1000000, 1)\n            \n            # EXIF data\n            exif_data = {}\n            if hasattr(img, '_getexif') and img._getexif():\n                for tag_id, value in img._getexif().items():\n                    tag = TAGS.get(tag_id, tag_id)\n                    if isinstance(value, bytes):\n                        try:\n                            value = value.decode()\n                        except:\n                            value = str(value)\n                    exif_data[tag] = value\n                \n                # Extract useful EXIF fields\n                if 'DateTime' in exif_data:\n                    metadata['datetime'] = exif_data['DateTime']\n                if 'Make' in exif_data:\n                    metadata['camera'] = exif_data['Make']\n                    if 'Model' in exif_data:\n                        metadata['camera'] += f\" {exif_data['Model']}\"\n            \n            # File stats\n            stat = os.stat(file_path)\n            metadata['size_mb'] = round(stat.st_size / (1024 * 1024), 2)\n            metadata['modified'] = datetime.fromtimestamp(stat.st_mtime).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n        \n        return metadata\n    except Exception as e:\n        return {\"error\": str(e)}\n\nmetadata = extract_image_metadata(\"$file\")\nfor key, value in metadata.items():\n    print(f\"{key}={value}\")\nEOF\n}\n\nsanitize_filename() {\n    echo \"$1\" | sed 's/[<>:\"/\\\\|?*]//g' | sed 's/^[[:space:]]*//;s/[[:space:]]*$//' | cut -c1-150\n}\n\norganize_images() {\n    local target_dir=\"${1:-.}\"\n    local dry_run=\"${2:-false}\"\n    \n    log_info \"Starting image organization in: $target_dir\"\n    \n    # Find all image files\n    find \"$target_dir\" -type f \\( \\\n        -iname \"*.jpg\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.jpeg\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.png\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.gif\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.webp\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.tiff\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.bmp\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.heic\" \\\n    \\) | while read -r file; do\n        filename=$(basename \"$file\")\n        extension=\"${filename##*.}\"\n        \n        log_info \"Processing: $filename\"\n        \n        # Extract image metadata\n        log_info \"Extracting image metadata...\"\n        while IFS='=' read -r key value; do\n            case \"$key\" in\n                size) dimensions=\"$value\" ;;\n                megapixels) megapixels=\"$value\" ;;\n                datetime) datetime=\"$value\" ;;\n                camera) camera=\"$value\" ;;\n                size_mb) size_mb=\"$value\" ;;\n            esac\n        done < <(extract_image_metadata \"$file\")\n        \n        # Try Gemini first, then OpenAI as fallback\n        new_name=$(analyze_image_with_gemini \"$file\")\n        \n        if [ $? -ne 0 ] || [ -z \"$new_name\" ] || [ \"$new_name\" = \"image_analysis_error\" ]; then\n            log_warning \"Gemini failed, trying OpenAI...\"\n            new_name=$(analyze_image_with_openai \"$file\")\n        fi\n        \n        if [ $? -eq 0 ] && [ -n \"$new_name\" ] && [ \"$new_name\" != \"openai_analysis_error\" ]; then\n            sanitized_name=$(sanitize_filename \"$new_name\")\n            new_filename=\"${sanitized_name}.${extension}\"\n            new_path=$(dirname \"$file\")/\"$new_filename\"\n            \n            # Handle duplicates\n            counter=1\n            while [ -f \"$new_path\" ]; do\n                name_part=\"${sanitized_name}\"\n                new_filename=\"${name_part}_${counter}.${extension}\"\n                new_path=$(dirname \"$file\")/\"$new_filename\"\n                counter=$((counter + 1))\n            done\n            \n            if [ \"$dry_run\" = \"true\" ]; then\n                log_info \"DRY RUN: Would rename '$filename' -> '$new_filename'\"\n                if [ -n \"$dimensions\" ]; then\n                    log_info \"Metadata: ${dimensions} (${megapixels}MP), Size: ${size_mb}MB\"\n                fi\n            else\n                mv \"$file\" \"$new_path\"\n                log_success \"Renamed: $filename -> $new_filename\"\n            fi\n        else\n            log_warning \"AI analysis failed for: $filename\"\n            # Create fallback name with metadata\n            if [ -n \"$datetime\" ]; then\n                fallback_name=\"image_${datetime}\"\n            else\n                fallback_name=\"image_${filename%.*}\"\n            fi\n            sanitized_name=$(sanitize_filename \"$fallback_name\")\n            new_filename=\"${sanitized_name}.${extension}\"\n            \n            if [ \"$dry_run\" = \"true\" ]; then\n                log_info \"DRY RUN: Would rename '$filename' -> '$new_filename' (fallback)\"\n            else\n                new_path=$(dirname \"$file\")/\"$new_filename\"\n                mv \"$file\" \"$new_path\"\n                log_success \"Renamed using fallback: $filename -> $new_filename\"\n            fi\n        fi\n    done\n    \n    log_success \"Image organization completed\"\n}\n\nmain() {\n    load_env\n    \n    local target_dir=\"${1:-.}\"\n    local dry_run=\"${2:-false}\"\n    \n    case \"$dry_run\" in\n        true|1|yes) dry_run=\"true\" ;;\n        *) dry_run=\"false\" ;;\n    esac\n    \n    organize_images \"$target_dir\" \"$dry_run\"\n}\n\nif [[ \"${BASH_SOURCE[0]}\" == \"${0}\" ]]; then\n    main \"$@\"\nfi\n```\n\n## 🔧 4. Environment Setup Script\n\n**`setup_environment.sh`**\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n\n# Setup script for file organization system\n\nset -e\n\nRED='\\033[0;31m'\nGREEN='\\033[0;32m'\nYELLOW='\\033[1;33m'\nNC='\\033[0m'\n\nlog_info() { echo -e \"${GREEN}[INFO]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_warning() { echo -e \"${YELLOW}[WARNING]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_error() { echo -e \"${RED}[ERROR]${NC} $1\"; }\n\ncheck_requirements() {\n    log_info \"Checking system requirements...\"\n    \n    # Check Python\n    if ! command -v python3 &> /dev/null; then\n        log_error \"Python3 is required but not installed\"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n    \n    # Check pip\n    if ! command -v pip3 &> /dev/null; then\n        log_error \"pip3 is required but not installed\"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n    \n    log_info \"System requirements satisfied\"\n}\n\nsetup_environment() {\n    log_info \"Setting up environment...\"\n    \n    # Create ~/.env if it doesn't exist\n    if [ ! You can now use the organization scripts.\"\n            ;;\n        *)\n            show_usage\n            ;;\n    esac\n}\n\nif [[ \"${BASH_SOURCE[0]}\" == \"${0}\" ]]; then\n    main \"$@\"\nfi\n```\n\n## 🚀 Usage Instructions\n\n1. **Setup the environment:**\n   ```bash\n   chmod +x setup_environment.sh\n   ./setup_environment.sh all\n   ```\n\n2. **Edit your ~/.env file** with your API keys\n\n3. **Run the organizers:**\n   ```bash\n   # Documents\n   ./organize_documents.sh /path/to/documents true  # Dry run\n   ./organize_documents.sh /path/to/documents       # Actual run\n   \n   # Audio/Video  \n   ./organize_audio_video.sh /path/to/media true\n   ./organize_audio_video.sh /path/to/media\n   \n   # Images\n   ./organize_images.sh /path/to/images true\n   ./organize_images.sh /path/to/images\n   ```\n\nEach script is specialized for its file type with appropriate APIs and metadata extraction, providing robust fallback options when AI analysis isn't available."
