Focus on the most distinctive elements.\nExamples: \n- \"Family-Christmas-2021-Santa-Hat\"\n- \"Ugly-Christmas-Sweater-Festive-Typography\" \n- \"Vintage-Christmas-Tree-Decorations\"\n- \"Christmas-Mug-Holiday-Greeting\"\n\"\"\"\n        \n        response = client.models.generate_content(\n            model=\"gemini-1.5-flash\",\n            contents=[prompt, uploaded_file]\n        )\n        return response.text.strip()\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"design_analysis_error: {str(e)}\")\n        return \"design_analysis_error\"\n\nresult = analyze_christmas_image(\"$file_path\")\nprint(result)\nEOF\n}\n\nextract_design_metadata() {\n    local file=\"$1\"\n    \n    python3 - << EOF\nimport os\nfrom PIL import Image\nfrom datetime import datetime\nimport re\n\ndef extract_design_metadata(file_path):\n    try:\n        metadata = {}\n        \n        with Image.open(file_path) as img:\n            # Basic image info\n            metadata['dimensions'] = f\"{img.width}x{img.height}\"\n            metadata['aspect_ratio'] = round(img.width / img.height, 2)\n            metadata['size_category'] = \"portrait\" if img.height > img.width else \"landscape\" if img.width > img.height else \"square\"\n            \n            # File stats\n            stat = os.stat(file_path)\n            file_size_mb = stat.st_size / (1024 * 1024)\n            metadata['size_mb'] = round(file_size_mb, 2)\n            metadata['created'] = datetime.fromtimestamp(stat.st_ctime).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n            \n            # Check if it's likely a design file vs photo\n            metadata['type'] = \"design\" if file_size_mb < 5 else \"photo\"\n            \n        return metadata\n    except Exception as e:\n        return {\"error\": str(e)}\n\nmetadata = extract_design_metadata(\"$file\")\nfor key, value in metadata.items():\n    print(f\"{key}={value}\")\nEOF\n}\n\ndetect_christmas_elements() {\n    local file=\"$1\"\n    \n    python3 - << EOF\nimport os\nfrom google import genai\n\ndef detect_christmas_theme(file_path):\n    try:\n        client = genai.Client(api_key=os.getenv('GOOGLE_API_KEY'))\n        uploaded_file = client.files.upload(file=file_path)\n        \n        prompt = \"\"\"\nQuickly identify if this image contains Christmas/holiday elements. \nRespond with a comma-separated list of main elements found, or \"none\" if no holiday elements.\nFocus on: Santa, Christmas trees, snowflakes, gifts, ornaments, holiday text, wreaths, snowmen, etc.\n\"\"\"\n        \n        response = client.models.generate_content(\n            model=\"gemini-1.5-flash\",\n            contents=[prompt, uploaded_file]\n        )\n        return response.text.strip()\n    except Exception as e:\n        return \"analysis_error\"\n\nresult = detect_christmas_theme(\"$file\")\nprint(result)\nEOF\n}\n\nsanitize_filename() {\n    echo \"$1\" | sed 's/[<>:\"/\\\\|?*]//g' | sed 's/^[[:space:]]*//;s/[[:space:]]*$//' | tr ' ' '-' | cut -c1-150\n}\n\ncategorize_christmas_image() {\n    local file=\"$1\"\n    local analysis_result=\"$2\"\n    \n    # Check if it's definitely Christmas-related\n    local christmas_elements=$(detect_christmas_elements \"$file\")\n    \n    if echo \"$christmas_elements\" | grep -i -q \"none\"; then\n        echo \"non-christmas\"\n    elif echo \"$analysis_result\" | grep -i -q \"christmas\\|holiday\\|santa\\|tree\\|snow\\|gift\\|ornament\\|wreath\"; then\n        echo \"christmas\"\n    else\n        echo \"unknown\"\n    fi\n}\n\norganize_christmas_images() {\n    local target_dir=\"${1:-.}\"\n    local dry_run=\"${2:-false}\"\n    local organize_by_type=\"${3:-true}\"\n    \n    log_info \"Starting Christmas image organization in: $target_dir\"\n    log_design \"Looking for holiday designs, typography, and Christmas graphics\"\n    \n    # Find all image files\n    find \"$target_dir\" -maxdepth 1 -type f \\( \\\n        -iname \"*.jpg\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.jpeg\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.png\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.gif\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.webp\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.tiff\" -o \\\n        -iname \"*.bmp\" \\\n    \\) | while read -r file; do\n        filename=$(basename \"$file\")\n        extension=\"${filename##*.}\"\n        base_name=$(basename \"$file\" \".$extension\")\n        \n        log_info \"Processing: $filename\"\n        \n        # Extract design metadata\n        log_design \"Analyzing design properties...\"\n        while IFS='=' read -r key value; do\n            case \"$key\" in\n                dimensions) dimensions=\"$value\" ;;\n                size_category) size_category=\"$value\" ;;\n                type) design_type=\"$value\" ;;\n                size_mb) size_mb=\"$value\" ;;\n            esac\n        done < <(extract_design_metadata \"$file\")\n        \n        # __init__(self, config: Config):\n        self.config = config\n        self.daily_spend = 0.0\n        self.costs_by_api = {\"google_vision\": 0.0, \"openai\": 0.0}\n        self.calls_by_api =        self.costs_by_api[api_name] += cost\n        self.calls_by_api[api_name] += 1\n        self.daily_spend += cost\n\n        # Check limits\n        max_daily = self.config.get(\"cost_limits\", \"max_daily_spend\")\n        warn_threshold = self.config.get(\"cost_limits\", \"warn_at_percentage\") / 100.0\n\n        if self.daily_spend > max_daily * warn_threshold:\n            self.logger.warning(f\"Daily spend warning: ${self.daily_spend:.2f} / ${max_daily:.2f}\")\n\n    def can_afford(self, api_name: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if we can afford another API call.\"\"\"\n        max_daily = self.config.get(\"cost_limits\", \"max_daily_spend\")\n        cost_per_call = self.config.get(\"cost_limits\", f\"{api_name}_cost_per_image\")\n        return (self.daily_spend + cost_per_call) <= max_daily\n\n    def get_summary(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Get cost summary.\"\"\"\n        return {\n            \"total_spend\": ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n# API CLIENT CLASSES\n# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n\n\nclass       self.cost_tracker = cost_tracker\n        self.client = vision.ImageAnnotatorClient()\n        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n    @backoff.on_exception(backoff.expo, Exception, max_tries=3, jitter=backoff.full_jitter)\n    def analyze_image(self, image_data: bytes) -> GoogleVisionResults:\n        \"\"\"Analyze image using Google Cloud Vision API.\"\"\"\n        if not self.cost_tracker.can_afford(\"google_vision\"):\n            raise Exception(\"Daily cost limit reached for Google Vision API\")\n\n        try:\n            image = vision.Image(content=image_data)\n            features = []\n\n            # Configure features based on config\n            for feature_type in self.config.get(\"google_vision\", \"features\"):\n                feature = vision.Feature(\n                    type_=getattr(vision.Feature.Type, feature_type),\n                    max_results=self.config.get(\"google_vision\", \"max_results\"),\n                )\n                features.append(feature)\n\n            # Make the API request\n            request = vision.AnnotateImageRequest(image=image, features=features)\n            response = self.client.annotate_image(request=request)\n\n            if response.error.message:\n                raise Exception(f\"Google Vision API error: {response.error.message}\")\n\n            # Record cost\n            cost = self.config.get(\"cost_limits\", \"google_vision_cost_per_image\")\n            self.cost_tracker.record_cost(\"google_vision\", cost)\n\n            # Parse response\n            return self._parse_response(response)\n\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.logger.error(f\"Google Vision API error: {e}\")\n            raise\n\n    def _parse_response(self, response) -> GoogleVisionResults:\n        \"\"\"Parse Google Vision API response into structured format.\"\"\"\n        results = GoogleVisionResults()\n\n        # Labels\n        if response.label_annotations:\n            results.labels = [\n                {\"description\": label.description, \"score\": label.score, \"confidence\": label.score}\n                for label in response.label_annotations\n                if label.score >= self.config.get(\"google_vision\", \"confidence_threshold\")\n            ]\n\n        # Objects\n        if response.localized_object_annotations:\n            results.objects = [\n                {\n                    \"name\": obj.name,\n                    \"score\": obj.score,\n                    \"bounding_box\": {\n                        \"vertices\": [(v.x, v.y) for v in obj.bounding_poly.normalized_vertices]\n                    },\n                }\n                for obj in response.localized_object_annotations\n            ]\n\n        # Colors\n        if response.image_properties_annotation:\n            results.colors = [\n                {\n                    \"color\": {\n                        \"red\": color.color.red,\n                        \"green\": color.color.green,\n                        \"blue\": color.color.blue,\n                    },\n                    \"score\": color.score,\n                    \"pixel_fraction\": color.pixel_fraction,\n                }\n                for color in response.image_properties_annotation.dominant_colors.colors\n            ]\n\n        # Text\n        if response.text_annotations:\n            results.text_annotations = [text.description for text in response.text_annotations]\n\n        # Safe search\n        if response.safe_search_annotation:\n            safe_search = response.safe_search_annotation\n            results.safe_search = {\n                \"adult\": safe_search.adult.name,\n                \"spoof\": safe_search.spoof.name,\n                \"medical\": safe_search.medical.name,\n                \"violence\": safe_search.violence.name,\n                \"racy\": safe_search.racy.name,\n            }\n\n        # Calculate overall confidence\n        if results.labels:\n            results.confidence = sum(label[\"score\"] for label in results.labels) / len(\n                results.labels\n            )\n\n        return results\n\n\nclass OpenAIClient:\n    \"\"\"OpenAI Vision API client optimized for semantic analysis.\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, config: Config, cost_tracker: CostTracker):\n        api_key = os.getenv(\"OPENAI_API_KEY\")\n        if not api_key:\n            raise ValueError(\"OPENAI_API_KEY environment variable not set\")\n\n        self.client = OpenAI(api_key=api_key)\n        self.config = config\n        self.cost_tracker = cost_tracker\n        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n    @backoff.on_exception(backoff.expo, Exception, max_tries=3, jitter=backoff.full_jitter)\n    def analyze_image(\n        self, image_data: str, mime_type: str, google_results: GoogleVisionResults = None\n    ) -> OpenAIResults:\n        \"\"\"Analyze image using OpenAI Vision API with context from Google Vision.\"\"\"\n        if not self.cost_tracker.can_afford(\"openai\"):\n            raise Exception(\"Daily cost limit reached for OpenAI API\")\n\n        try:\n            # Build context from Google Vision results\n            context = self._build_context_from_google(google_results) if google_results else \"\"\n\n            messages = [\n                {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": self.config.get(\"prompts\", \"openai_system\")},\n                {\n                    \"role\": \"user\",\n                    \"content\": [\n                        {\n                            \"type\": \"image_url\",\n                            \"image_url\": {\n                                \"url\": f\"data:{mime_type};base64,{image_data}\",\n                                \"detail\": \"high\",\n                            },\n                        },\n                        {\n                            \"type\": \"text\",\n                            \"text\": f\"{context}\\n\\n{self.config.get('prompts', 'openai_user')}\",\n                        },\n                    ],\n                },\n            ]\n\n            response = self.client.chat.completions.create(\n                model=self.config.get(\"openai\", \"model\"),\n                messages=messages,\n                max_tokens=self.config.get(\"openai\", \"max_tokens\"),\n                temperature=self.config.get(\"openai\", \"temperature\"),\n            )\n\n            # Record cost\n            cost = self.config.get(\"cost_limits\", \"openai_cost_per_image\")\n            self.cost_tracker.record_cost(\"openai\", cost)\n\n            content = response.choices[0].message.content\n            return self._parse_response(content)\n\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.logger.error(f\"OpenAI API error: {e}\")\n            raise\n\n    def _build_context_from_google(self, google_results: GoogleVisionResults) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Build context string from Google Vision results.\"\"\"\n        context_parts = []\n\n        if google_results.labels:\n            labels = [label[\"description\"] for label in google_results.labels[:5]]\n            context_parts.append(f\"Detected objects/concepts: {', '.join(labels)}\")\n\n        if google_results.colors:\n            dominant_colors = google_results.colors[:3]\n            color_descriptions = [\n                f\"RGB({c['color']['red']}, {c['color']['green']}, {c['color']['blue']})\"\n                for c in dominant_colors\n            ]\n            context_parts.append(f\"Dominant colors: {', '.join(color_descriptions)}\")\n\n        if google_results.safe_search:\n            safety_info = [f\"{k}: {v}\" for k, v in google_results.safe_search.items()]\n            context_parts.append(f\"Safety ratings: {', '.join(safety_info)}\")\n\n        return (\n            \"Context from technical analysis:\\n\" + \"\\n\".join(context_parts) if context_parts else \"\"\n        )\n\n    def _parse_response(self, content: str) -> OpenAIResults:\n        \"\"\"Parse OpenAI response into structured format.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            start_idx = content.find(\"{\")\n            end_idx = content.rfind(\"}\") + 1\n\n            if start_idx == -1 or end_idx == 0:\n                raise ValueError(\"No JSON object found in response\")\n\n            json_str = content[start_idx:end_idx]\n            data = json.loads(json_str)\n\n            return OpenAIResults(\n                style_description=data.get(\"style\"),\n                emotional_context=data.get(\"emotion\"),\n                marketing_copy=data.get(\"brand_alignment\"),\n                seo_title=data.get(\"seo_title\"),\n                seo_description=data.get(\"seo_description\"),\n                target_audience=data.get(\"target_audience\"),\n                brand_alignment=data.get(\"brand_alignment\"),\n                confidence=data.get(\"confidence_score\", 0.0),\n            )\n\n        except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError) as e:\n            self.logger.warning(f\"OpenAI JSON parsing failed: {e}\")\n            return OpenAIResults()\n\n\n# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n# MAIN PROCESSING CLASS\n# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n\n\nclass HybridImageProcessor:\n    \"\"\"Main processor that combines Google Vision and OpenAI for optimal results.\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, config: Config):\n        self.config = config\n        self.cost_tracker = CostTracker(config)\n        self.google_client = GoogleVisionClient(config, self.cost_tracker)\n        self.openai_client = OpenAIClient(config, self.cost_tracker)\n        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n        self.valid_extensions = set(self.config.get(\"image\", \"valid_extensions\"))\n\n    def discover_images(self, input_folder: Path) -> List[Path]:\n        \"\"\"Recursively find all valid image files.\"\"\"\n        image_files = []\n\n        for root, _, files in os.walk(input_folder):\n            root_path = Path(root)\n            for filename in files:\n                file_path = root_path / filename\n                if file_path.suffix.lower() in self.valid_extensions:\n                    # Check file size\n                    max_size = self.config.get(\"image\", \"max_size_mb\") * 1024 * 1024\n                    if file_path.stat().st_size <= max_size:\n                        image_files.append(file_path)\n                    else:\n                        self.logger.warning(f\"Skipping large file: {filename}\")\n\n        return sorted(image_files)\n\n    def extract_metadata(self, image_path: Path) -> ImageMetadata:\n        \"\"\"Extract technical metadata from image file.\"\"\"\n        metadata = ImageMetadata(filename=image_path.name)\n\n        try:\n            with Image.open(image_path) as img:\n                metadata.width = img.width\n                metadata.height = img.height\n                metadata.format = img.format\n                metadata.aspect_ratio = round(img.width / img.height, 2) if img.height > 0 else None\n\n                # Extract DPI information\n                dpi_info = img.info.get(\"dpi\", (300, 300))\n                metadata.dpi = dpi_info[0] if isinstance(dpi_info, tuple) else dpi_info\n\n            # File system metadata\n            stat = image_path.stat()\n            metadata.file_size = stat.st_size\n            metadata.created_date = datetime.fromtimestamp(stat.st_ctime).strftime(\n                \"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\"\n            )\n\n        except UnidentifiedImageError:\n            self.logger.warning(f\"Cannot identify image format: {image_path.name}\")\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.logger.error(f\"Error extracting metadata for {image_path.name}: {e}\")\n\n        return metadata\n\n    def process_single_image(self, image_path: Path, base_folder: Path) -> ProcessingResult:\n        \"\"\"Process a single image using hybrid approach.\"\"\"\n        start_time = time.time()\n\n        try:\n            # Extract metadata\n            metadata = self.extract_metadata(image_path)\n\n            # Load and prepare image data\n            image_data = self._load_image_data(image_path)\n\n            # Step 1: Always run Google Vision for technical analysis\n            google_results = GoogleVisionResults()\n            if self.config.get(\"google_vision\", \"enabled\"):\n                google_results = self.google_client.analyze_image(image_data)\n\n            # Step 2: Determine if OpenAI analysis is needed\n            openai_results = OpenAIResults()\n            if self._should_use_openai(google_results, metadata):\n                if self.config.get(\"openai\", \"enabled\"):\n                    # Encode for OpenAI\n                    image_b64, mime_type = self._encode_for_openai(image_path)\n                    openai_results = self.openai_client.analyze_image(\n                        image_b64, mime_type, google_results\n                    )\n\n            # Step 3: Combine results\n            combined_analysis = self._combine_results(google_results, openai_results, metadata)\n\n            # Generate source tag\n            source_tag = self._build_source_tag(image_path, base_folder)\n\n            processing_time = time.time() - start_time\n\n            return ProcessingResult(\n                image_path=image_path,\n                metadata=metadata,\n                google_results=google_results,\n                openai_results=openai_results,\n                combined_analysis=combined_analysis,\n                source_tag=source_tag,\n                processing_time=processing_time,\n                success=True,\n                api_costs=self.cost_tracker.costs_by_api.copy(),\n            )\n\n        except Exception as e:\n            processing_time = time.time() - start_time\n            self.logger.error(f\"Error processing {image_path.name}: {e}\")\n\n            return ProcessingResult(\n                image_path=image_path,\n                metadata=ImageMetadata(filename=image_path.name),\n                google_results=GoogleVisionResults(),\n                openai_results=OpenAIResults(),\n                combined_analysis=CombinedAnalysis(),\n                source_tag=\"\",\n                processing_time=processing_time,\n                success=False,\n                error_message=str(e),\n                api_costs=self.cost_tracker.costs_by_api.copy(),\n            )\n\n    def _load_image_data(self, image_path: Path) -> bytes:\n        \"\"\"Load image data, optionally resizing if too large.\"\"\"\n        with open(image_path, \"rb\") as f:\n            data = f.read()\n\n        # Check if resizing is needed and enabled\n        if self.config.get(\"image\", \"resize_large_images\"):\n            try:\n                img = Image.open(BytesIO(data))\n                max_dim = self.config.get(\"image\", \"max_dimension\")\n\n                if max(img.width, img.height) > max_dim:\n                    # Calculate new dimensions maintaining aspect ratio\n                    if img.width > img.height:\n                        new_width = max_dim\n                        new_height = int((max_dim * img.height) / img.width)\n                    else:\n                        new_height = max_dim\n                        new_width = int((max_dim * img.width) / img.height)\n\n                    img = img.resize((new_width, new_height), Image.Resampling.LANCZOS)\n\n                    # Convert back to bytes\n                    buffer = BytesIO()\n                    img.save(buffer, format=img.format or \"JPEG\", quality=85)\n                    data = buffer.getvalue()\n\n                    self.logger.info(f\"Resized {image_path.name} to {new_width}x{new_height}\")\n\n            except Exception as e:\n                self.logger.warning(f\"Failed to resize {image_path.name}: {e}\")\n\n        return data\n\n    def _encode_for_openai(self, image_path: Path) -> Tuple[str, str]:\n        \"\"\"Encode image for OpenAI API.\"\"\"\n        with open(image_path, \"rb\") as image_file:\n            encoded_string = base64.b64encode(image_file.read()).decode(\"utf-8\")\n\n        # Determine MIME type\n        ext = image_path.suffix.lower()\n        mime_map = {\n            \".jpg\": \"image/jpeg\",\n            \".jpeg\": \"image/jpeg\",\n            \".png\": \"image/png\",\n            \".gif\": \"image/gif\",\n            \".bmp\": \"image/bmp\",\n            \".tiff\": \"image/tiff\",\n            \".webp\": \"image/webp\",\n        }\n        mime_type = mime_map.get(ext, \"image/jpeg\")\n\n        return encoded_string, mime_type\n\n    def _should_use_openai(\n        self, google_results: GoogleVisionResults, metadata: ImageMetadata\n    ) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Determine if OpenAI analysis is needed based on complexity and configuration.\"\"\"\n        if not self.config.get(\"processing\", \"use_openai_only_when_needed\"):\n            return True\n\n        # Always use OpenAI if it's the only enabled API\n        if not self.config.get(\"google_vision\", \"enabled\"):\n            return True\n\n        # Check for complexity indicators\n        complexity_indicators = self.config.get(\"analysis_rules\", \"complexity_indicators\")\n\n        # Analyze Google results for complexity\n        if google_results.labels:\n            labels = [label[\"description\"].lower() for label in google_results.labels]\n\n            # Check for artistic or abstract content\n            artistic_terms = [\n                \"art\",\n                \"painting\",\n                \"drawing\",\n                \"abstract\",\n                \"artistic\",\n                \"creative\",\n                \"design\",\n            ]\n            if any(term in \" \".join(labels) for term in artistic_terms):\n                return True\n\n            # Check confidence - low confidence might need OpenAI\n            if google_results.confidence < 0.7:\n                return True\n\n        # Check image properties for complexity\n        if metadata.aspect_ratio and (metadata.aspect_ratio < 0.5 or metadata.aspect_ratio > 2.0):\n            return True  # Unusual aspect ratios might be artistic\n\n        # Default: use Google Vision only for straightforward images\n        return False\n\n    def _combine_results(\n        self,\n        google_results: GoogleVisionResults,\n        openai_results: OpenAIResults,\n        metadata: ImageMetadata,\n    ) -> CombinedAnalysis:\n        \"\"\"Combine results from both APIs into unified analysis.\"\"\"\n        analysis = CombinedAnalysis()\n\n        # From Google Vision\n        if google_results.labels:\n            analysis.primary_objects = [label[\"description\"] for label in google_results.labels[:5]]\n\n        if google_results.colors:\n            analysis.color_palette = [\n                f\"#{int(c['color']['red']):02x}{int(c['color']['green']):02x}{int(c['color']['blue']):02x}\"\n                for c in google_results.colors[:5]\n            ]\n\n        if google_results.text_annotations:\n            analysis.detected_text = \" \".join(google_results.text_annotations[:3])\n\n        if google_results.safe_search:\n            # Convert to simple safety rating\n            adult = google_results.safe_search.get(\"adult\", \"UNKNOWN\")\n            if adult in [\"VERY_UNLIKELY\", \"UNLIKELY\"]:\n                analysis.safety_rating = \"G\"\n            elif adult == \"POSSIBLE\":\n                analysis.safety_rating = \"PG\"\n            else:\n                analysis.safety_rating = \"R\"\n\n        # From OpenAI (if available)\n        if openai_results.style_description:\n            analysis.style = openai_results.style_description\n        if openai_results.emotional_context:\n            analysis.emotion = openai_results.emotional_context\n        if openai_results.seo_title:\n            analysis.seo_title = openai_results.seo_title\n        if openai_results.seo_description:\n            analysis.seo_description = openai_results.seo_description\n\n        # Generate suggested products from both sources\n        products = []\n        if google_results.labels:\n            # Map labels to product categories\n            label_to_product = {\n                \"clothing\": [\"T-Shirt\", \"Hoodie\", \"Tank Top\"],\n                \"art\": [\"Canvas Print\", \"Poster\", \"Sticker\"],\n                \"nature\": [\"Calendar\", \"Postcard\", \"Wall Art\"],\n                \"food\": [\"Kitchen Towel\", \"Apron\", \"Coaster\"],\n                \"technology\": [\"Phone Case\", \"Laptop Sticker\", \"Mouse Pad\"],\n                \"animal\": [\"Pet Accessories\", \"Plush Toy\", \"Mug\"],\n                \"vehicle\": [\"Bumper Sticker\", \"License Plate\", \"Keychain\"],\n            }\n\n            for label in google_results.labels[:3]:\n                desc = label[\"description\"].lower()\n                for category, items in label_to_product.items():\n                    if category in desc:\n                        products.extend(items[:2])\n                        break\n\n        analysis.suggested_products = list(set(products[:5]))  # Remove duplicates, limit to 5\n\n        # Generate dominant keyword\n        if analysis.primary_objects:\n            analysis.dominant_keyword = analysis.primary_objects[0]\n\n        # Calculate overall confidence\n        confidences = []\n        if google_results.confidence > 0:\n            confidences.append(google_results.confidence)\n        if openai_results.confidence > 0:\n            confidences.append(openai_results.confidence)\n\n        analysis.overall_confidence = sum(confidences) / len(confidences) if confidences else 0.0\n\n        # Calculate processing cost\n        analysis.processing_cost = sum(self.cost_tracker.costs_by_api.values())\n\n        return analysis\n\n    def _build_source_tag(self, image_path: Path, base_folder: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Generate source tag for the image.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            relative_path = image_path.relative_to(base_folder)\n            parent_parts = relative_path.parent.parts\n            folder_id = \"-\".join(parent_parts) if parent_parts else base_folder.name\n            date_str = datetime.now().strftime(\"%Y%m%d\")\n            return f\"{folder_id}-{date_str}\"\n        except ValueError:\n            return f\"{base_folder.name}-{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')}\"\n\n\nclass CSVWriter:\n    \"\"\"Enhanced CSV writer for hybrid results.\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, output_path: Path, config: Config):\n        self.output_path = output_path\n        self.config = config\n        self.fieldnames = self._get_fieldnames()\n\n    def _get_fieldnames(self) -> List[str]:\n        \"\"\"Define CSV column headers for hybrid results.\"\"\"\n        return [\n            # Technical metadata\n            \"filename\",\n            \"width\",\n            \"height\",\n            \"dpi\",\n            \"format\",\n            \"file_size\",\n            \"created_date\",\n            \"aspect_ratio\",\n            # Combined analysis results\n            \"primary_objects\",\n            \"color_palette\",\n            \"detected_text\",\n            \"safety_rating\",\n            \"style\",\n            \"emotion\",\n            \"suggested_products\",\n            \"seo_title\",\n            \"seo_description\",\n            \"dominant_keyword\",\n            \"overall_confidence\",\n            # Processing metadata\n            \"source_tag\",\n            \"processing_time\",\n            \"success\",\n            \"error_message\",\n            \"google_vision_used\",\n            \"openai_used\",\n            \"processing_cost\",\n            # Raw API results (optional)\n            \"google_labels\",\n            \"google_objects\",\n            \"google_colors\",\n            \"openai_style\",\n            \"openai_emotion\",\n            \"openai_target_audience\",\n            # Cost tracking\n            \"google_vision_cost\",\n            \"openai_cost\",\n            \"total_api_cost\",\n        ]\n\n    def write_results(self, results: List[ProcessingResult], cost_summary: Dict[str, Any]):\n        \"\"\"Write processing results to CSV with cost summary.\"\"\"\n        with open(self.output_path, \"w\", newline=\"\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as csvfile:\n            writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=self.fieldnames)\n            writer.writeheader()\n\n            for result in results:\n                row = self._result_to_row(result)\n                writer.writerow(row)\n\n        # Write cost summary to separate file\n        cost_file = self.output_path.parent / f\"{self.output_path.stem}_cost_summary.json\"\n        with open(cost_file, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            json.dump(cost_summary, f, indent=2)\n\n    def _result_to_row(self, result: ProcessingResult) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Convert ProcessingResult to CSV row.\"\"\"\n        ca = result.combined_analysis\n\n        row = {\n            # Technical metadata\n            \"filename\": result.metadata.filename,\n            \"width\": result.metadata.width,\n            \"height\": result.metadata.height,\n            \"dpi\": result.metadata.dpi,\n            \"format\": result.metadata.format,\n            \"file_size\": result.metadata.file_size,\n            \"created_date\": result.metadata.created_date,\n            \"aspect_ratio\": result.metadata.aspect_ratio,\n            # Combined analysis\n            \"primary_objects\": json.dumps(ca.primary_objects) if ca.primary_objects else \"[]\",\n            \"color_palette\": json.dumps(ca.color_palette) if ca.color_palette else \"[]\",\n            \"detected_text\": ca.detected_text or \"\",\n            \"safety_rating\": ca.safety_rating or \"\",\n            \"style\": ca.style or \"\",\n            \"emotion\": ca.emotion or \"\",\n            \"suggested_products\": (\n                json.dumps(ca.suggested_products) if ca.suggested_products else \"[]\"\n            ),\n            \"seo_title\": ca.seo_title or \"\",\n            \"seo_description\": ca.seo_description or \"\",\n            \"dominant_keyword\": ca.dominant_keyword or \"\",\n            \"overall_confidence\": ca.overall_confidence,\n            # Processing metadata\n            \"source_tag\": result.source_tag,\n            \"processing_time\": round(result.processing_time, 2),\n            \"success\": result.success,\n            \"error_message\": result.error_message or \"\",\n            \"google_vision_used\": bool(\n                result.google_results.labels or result.google_results.objects\n            ),\n            \"openai_used\": bool(\n                result.openai_results.style_description or result.openai_results.seo_title\n            ),\n            \"processing_cost\": ca.processing_cost,\n            # Raw API results\n            \"google_labels\": json.dumps(\n                [l[\"description\"] for l in (result.google_results.labels or [])]\n            ),\n            \"google_objects\": json.dumps(\n                [o[\"name\"] for o in (result.google_results.objects or [])]\n            ),\n            \"google_colors\": json.dumps(result.google_results.colors or []),\n            \"openai_style\": result.openai_results.style_description or \"\",\n            \"openai_emotion\": result.openai_results.emotional_context or \"\",\n            \"openai_target_audience\": result.openai_results.target_audience or \"\",\n            # Cost tracking\n            \"google_vision_cost\": (\n                result.api_costs.get(\"google_vision\", 0.0) if result.api_costs else 0.0\n            ),\n            \"openai_cost\": result.api_costs.get(\"openai\", 0.0) if result.api_costs else 0.0,\n            \"total_api_cost\": sum(result.api_costs.values()) if result.api_costs else 0.0,\n        }\n\n        return row\n\n\n# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n# MAIN PIPELINE CLASS\n# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n\n\nclass HybridImagePipeline:\n    \"\"\"Main pipeline orchestrator for hybrid analysis.\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, config_path: Optional[Path] = None):\n        self.config = Config(config_path)\n        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n        self.processor = HybridImageProcessor(self.config)\n\n    def run(self, input_folder: Path, output_csv: Path) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Run the hybrid image analysis pipeline.\"\"\"\n        start_time = time.time()\n\n        try:\n            # Discover images\n            self.logger.info(f\"Scanning for images in: {input_folder}\")\n            image_paths = self.processor.discover_images(input_folder)\n\n            if not image_paths:\n                self.logger.warning(\"No valid images found\")\n                return False\n\n            self.logger.info(f\"Found {len(image_paths)} images to process\")\n\n            # Process images\n            max_workers = self.config.get(\"processing\", \"max_workers\")\n\n            if max_workers > 1:\n                results = self._process_concurrent(image_paths, input_folder, max_workers)\n            else:\n                results = self._process_sequential(image_paths, input_folder)\n\n            # Get cost summary\n            cost_summary = self.processor.cost_tracker.get_summary()\n\n            # Write results\n            self.logger.info(f\"Writing results to: {output_csv}\")\n            writer = CSVWriter(output_csv, self.config)\n            writer.write_results(results, cost_summary)\n\n            # Summary statistics\n            successful = sum(1 for r in results if r.success)\n            google_used = sum(1 for r in results if r.google_results.labels)\n            openai_used = sum(1 for r in results if r.openai_results.seo_title)\n            total_time = time.time() - start_time\n            avg_time = sum(r.processing_time for r in results) / len(results) if results else 0\n\n            self.logger.info(\"=\" * 60)\n            self.logger.info(\"HYBRID PIPELINE COMPLETE!\")\n            self.logger.info(\"=\" * 60)\n            self.logger.info(f\"Images processed: {successful}/{len(results)} successfully\")\n            self.logger.info(f\"Google Vision used: {google_used} times\")\n            self.logger.info(f\"OpenAI used: {openai_used} times\")\n            self.logger.info(f\"Total cost:    except KeyboardInterrupt:\n            self.logger.warning(\"Pipeline interrupted by user\")\n            return False\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.logger.error(f\"Pipeline failed: {e}\")\n            return False\n\n    def _process_sequential(\n        self, image_paths: List[Path], base_folder: Path\n    ) -> List[ProcessingResult]:\n        \"\"\"Process images sequentially.\"\"\"\n        results = []\n\n        with tqdm(image_paths, desc=\"Processing images\", unit=\"image\") as pbar:\n            for image_path in pbar:\n                pbar.set_postfix({\"current\": image_path.name})\n                result = self.processor.process_single_image(image_path, base_folder)\n                results.append(result)\n\n                # Update progress bar with cost info\n                cost_so_far = self.processor.cost_tracker.daily_spend\n                pbar.set_postfix({\"current\": image_path.name, \"cost\": f\"${cost_so_far:.3f}\"})\n\n                if not result.success:\n                    self.logger.warning(f\"Failed to process: {image_path.name}\")\n\n        return results\n\n    def _process_concurrent(\n        self, image_paths: List[Path], base_folder: Path, max_workers: int\n    ) -> List[ProcessingResult]:\n        \"\"\"Process images concurrently with thread pool.\"\"\"\n        results = []\n\n        with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=max_workers) as executor:\n            # Submit all tasks\n            future_to_path = {\n                executor.submit(self.processor.process_single_image, path, base_folder): path\n                for path in image_paths\n            }\n\n            # Process completed tasks with progress bar\n            with tqdm(total=len(image_paths), desc=\"Processing images\", unit=\"image\") as pbar:\n                for future in as_completed(future_to_path):\n                    image_path = future_to_path[future]\n                    try:\n                        result = future.result()\n                        results.append(result)\n\n                        cost_so_far = self.processor.cost_tracker.daily_spend\n                        if result.success:\n                            pbar.set_postfix(\n                                {\"completed\": image_path.name, \"cost\": f\"${cost_so_far:.3f}\"}\n                            )\n                        else:\n                            pbar.set_postfix(\n                                {\"failed\": image_path.name, \"cost\": f\"${cost_so_far:.3f}\"}\n                            )\n\n                    except Exception as e:\n                        self.logger.error(f\"Unexpected error processing {image_path.name}: {e}\")\n                        failed_result = ProcessingResult(\n                            image_path=image_path,\n                            metadata=ImageMetadata(filename=image_path.name),\n                            google_results=GoogleVisionResults(),\n                            openai_results=OpenAIResults(),\n                            combined_analysis=CombinedAnalysis(),\n                            source_tag=\"\",\n                            processing_time=0.0,\n                            success=False,\n                            error_message=str(e),\n                        )\n                        results.append(failed_result)\n\n                    pbar.update(1)\n\n        # Sort results by original order\n        path_to_result = {r.image_path: r for r in results}\n        return [path_to_result[path] for path in image_paths if path in path_to_result]\n\n\n# 'original_path': file_path,\n                'error': str(e),\n                'processing_time': time.time() - start_time\n            }\n\n    def _extract_document_metadata(self, file_path: Path)         filename=file_path.name,\n            file_size=stat.st_size,\n            file_type=file_path.suffix.lower(),\n = None\n    scene_changes: int = 0\n    \n    # SEO/Marketing\n    seo_title: str\n    seo_description: str\n    target_platforms: List[str]\n    tags: List[str]\n    \n    confidence: float =   'audio': {'.mp3', '.wav', '.m4a', '.flac', '.aac', '.ogg'},\n            'video': {'.mp4', '.avi', '.mov', '.mkv', '.wmv', '.flv'}\n        }\n\n    def extract_media_metadata(self, file_path: Path) media_info.audio_tracks else None\n            video_track = media_info.video_tracks[0] if media_info.video_tracks else None\n            \n            return MediaMetadata(\n                filename=file_path.name,\n                file_size=file_path.stat().st_size,\n                duration=float(general_track.duration) / 1000 if general_track and general_track.duration else 0,\n                format=file_path.suffix.lower(),\n                bitrate=int(general_track.bitrate) if general_track and general_track.bitrate else None,\n MediaMetadata(\n                filename=file_path.name,\n                file_size=file_path.stat().st_size,\n                duration=0,\n                format=file_path.suffix.lower()\n            )\n\n    def transcribe_audio(self, file_path: Path) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Transcribe audio content using OpenAI Whisper.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            # This would use OpenAI's Whisper API\n            # For now, return placeholder\n            return \"Audio transcription placeholder\"\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            self.logger.error(f\"Audio transcription failed: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def analyze_with_openai(self, file_path: Path, media_type: str, \n                          transcription: str = None) -> MediaAnalysis:\n        \"\"\"Use OpenAI for comprehensive media analysis.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            if media_type == 'audio' and transcription:\n                prompt = f\"\"\"\n                Analyze this audio content and provide comprehensive analysis:\n                \n                TRANSCRIPTION:\n                {transcription}\n                \n                Please analyze:\n                1. Main topics and themes discussed\n                2. Overall sentiment and mood\n                3. Number of speakers (if detectable)\n                4. Key moments or important points\n                5. Content summary\n                6. SEO-optimized title\n                7. SEO-optimized description\n                8. Target platforms (podcast, music, etc.)\n                9. Relevant tags\n                \n                Return as JSON.\n                \"\"\"\n            else:\n                prompt = f\"\"\"\n                Analyze this {media_type} file and provide comprehensive analysis.\n                Focus on content, mood, and potential use cases.\n                \n                Please provide:\n                1. Content summary\n                2. Main themes/topics\n                3. Sentiment and mood\n                4. Key moments/scenes\n                5. Visual elements (for video)\n                6. SEO-optimized title\n                7. SEO-optimized description\n                8. Target platforms\n                9. Relevant tags\n                \n                Return as JSON.\n                \"\"\"\n            \n            # Upload file to OpenAI for analysis\n            uploaded_file = self.openai_client.files.upload(file=file_path)\n            response = self.openai_client.analyze_media(uploaded_file, prompt)\n            data = json.loads(response)\n            \n            return MediaAnalysis(\n                media_type=media_type,\n                content_summary=data.get('content_summary', ''),\n                main_topics=data.get('main_topics', []),\n                sentiment=data.get('sentiment', 'neutral'),\n                mood=data.get('mood', ''),\n                key_moments=data.get('key_moments', []),\n                transcription=transcription,\n                visual_elements=data.get('visual_elements', []),\n                seo_title=data.get('seo_title', ''),\n                seo_description=data.get('seo_description', ''),\n                target_platforms=data.get('target_platforms', []),\n                tags=data.get('tags', []),\n                confidence=data.get('confidence', 0.0)\n            )\n            \n        except             target_platforms=[],\n                tags=[],\n                confidence=0.0\n            )\n\n    def generate_filename(self, analysis: MediaAnalysis, metadata: MediaMetadata) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Generate descriptive filename from media analysis.\"\"\"\n        import re\n        from datetime import datetime\n        \n        # Use content summary and main topics\n        if analysis.content_summary:\n            base_name = analysis.content_summary.split('.')[0]\n        else:\n            base_name = f\"{analysis.media_type}-file\"\n        \n        # Add key elements\n        if analysis.main_topics:\n            topics = '-'.join(analysis.main_topics[:2])\n            base_name = f\"{base_name}-{topics}\"\n        \n        # Add duration for media files\n        if metadata.duration > 0:\n            minutes = int(metadata.duration // 60)\n            base_name = f\"{base_name}-{minutes}min\"\n        \n        # Clean and sanitize\n        clean_name = re.sub(r'[^\\w\\s-]', '', base_name)\n        clean_name = re.sub(r'[-\\s]+', '-', clean_name)\n        clean_name = clean_name.strip('-').lower()\n        \n        return clean_name[:100]\n\n    def process_media_file(self, file_path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Process a single media file.\"\"\"\n        import time\n        start_time = time.time()\n        \n        try:\n            # Determine media type\n            media_type = 'video' if file_path.suffix.lower() in self.supported_extensions['video'] else 'audio'\n            \n            # Extract metadata\n            metadata = self.extract_media_metadata(file_path)\n            \n            # Transcribe audio if applicable\n            transcription = None\n            if media_type == 'audio':\n                transcription = self.transcribe_audio(file_path)\n            \n            # Analyze content\n            analysis = self.analyze_with_openai(file_path, media_type, transcription)\n            \n            # Generate filename\n            new_filename = self.generate_filename(analysis, metadata)\n            \n            processing_time = time.time() - start_time\n            \n            return {\n                'success': True,\n                'original_path': file_path,\n                'new_filename': new_filename,\n                'metadata': metadata,\n                'analysis': analysis,\n                'processing_time': processing_time,\n                'media_type': media_type,\n                'file_extension': file_path.suffix\n            }\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            self.logger.error(f\"Media processing failed: {e}\")\n            return {\n                'success': False,\n                'original_path': file_path,\n                'error': str(e),\n                'processing_time': time.time() - start_time\n            }\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Main entry containing media files\")\n    parser.add_argument(\"-o\", \"--output\", type=Path, default=Path(\"media_analysis.csv\"))\n    parser.add_argument(\"--config\", type=Path, help=\"Configuration file\")\n    \n    args = parser.parse_args()\n    \n    setup_logging(Path(\"av_pipeline.log\"), \"INFO\")\n    config = Config(args.config)\n    processor = EnhancedAVProcessor(config)\n    \n    # Process media files\n    results = []\n    for pattern in ['*.*']:  # Would iterate through supported extensions\n        for file_path in args.input_folder.rglob(pattern):\n            ext = file_path.suffix.lower()\n            if (ext in processor.supported_extensions['audio'] or \n                ext in processor.supported_extensions['video']):\n                result = processor.process_media_file(file_path)\n                results.append(result)\n    \n    # Save results and print summary\n    successful = sum(1 for r in results if r['success'])\n main()\n```\n\n### 3. **Unified File Organizer** (`unified_file_organizer.py`)\n\n```python\n#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nUnified File Organization System\n================================\nOrchestrates all specialized processors for comprehensive file organization.\nIntegrates with your enhanced image pipeline architecture.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport argparse\nimport os\nimport sys\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\nimport logging\nfrom concurrent.futures import EnhancedDocumentProcessor\nfrom enhanced_av_processor import EnhancedAVProcessor\n\n@dataclass\nclass OrganizationResult:\n    \"\"\"Result of file organization operation.\"\"\"\n    original_path: Path\n    new_path: Path\n    file_type: str\n    success: bool\n    error: Optional[str] = None\n    processing_time: float = 0.0\n    analysis_data: Optional[Dict] = None\n\nclass UnifiedFileOrganizer:\n    \"\"\"Main orchestrator for all file organization tasks.\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, config_path: Optional[Path] = None):\n        self.config_path = config_path\n        self.setup_logging()\n        self.load_config()\n        self.initialize_processors()\n        \n    def setup_logging(self):\n        \"\"\"Setup comprehensive logging.\"\"\"\n \n    def load_config(self):\n        \"\"\"Load unified configuration.\"\"\"\n        # This would load from your enhanced config system\n        self.config = {\n            'processing': {\n                'max_workers': 4,\n                'batch_size': 10,\n                'dry_run': False\n            },\n            'organize_by_type': True,\n            'backup_original': True,\n            'cost_limits': {\n                'max_daily_spend': 50.0\n            }\n        }\n        \n    def initialize_processors(self):\n        \"\"\"Initialize all specialized processors.\"\"\"\n        self.logger.info(\"Initializing specialized processors...\")\n        \n        # Image processor (your existing enhanced pipeline)\n        self.image_processor = HybridImagePipeline(self.config_path)\n        \n        # Document processor\n        self.document_processor = EnhancedDocumentProcessor(self.config_path)\n        \n        # Audio/Video processor  \n        self.av_processor = EnhancedAVProcessor(self.config_path)\n        \n        self.logger.info(\"All processors initialized successfully\")\n        \n    def organize_files(self, input_folder: Path, output_base: Path, \n                      file_types: List[str] = None, dry_run: bool = False) -> List[OrganizationResult]:\n        \"\"\"Organize all files in the input folder.\"\"\"\n        if file_types is None:\n            file_types = ['images', 'documents', 'audio', 'video']\n            \n        results = []\n        \n        with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=self.config['processing']['max_workers']) as executor:\n            futures = []\n            \n            # Submit organization tasks for each file type\n            if 'images' in file_types:\n                futures.append(executor.submit(self._organize_images, input_folder, output_base, dry_run))\n            if 'documents' in file_types:\n                futures.append(executor.submit(self._organize_documents, input_folder, output_base, dry_run))\n            if 'audio' in file_types:\n                futures.append(executor.submit(self._organize_audio, input_folder, output_base, dry_run))\n            if 'video' in file_types:\n                futures.append(executor.submit(self._organize_video, input_folder, output_base, dry_run))\n                \n            # Collect results\n            for future in as_completed(futures):\n                try:\n                    batch_results = future.result()\n                    results.extend(batch_results)\n                except Exception as e:\n                    self.logger.error(f\"Organization batch failed: {e}\")\n                    \n        return results\n        \n    def _organize_images(self, input_folder: Path, output_base: Path, dry_run: bool) -> List[OrganizationResult]:\n        \"\"\"Organize image files using enhanced pipeline.\"\"\"\n        results = []\n        \n        # Use your existing image pipeline\n        output_csv = output_base / \"image_analysis.csv\"\n        success = self.image_processor.run(input_folder, output_csv)\n        \n        if success:\n            # Process results and organize files\n            # This would read the CSV and perform actual file organization\n            pass\n            \n        return results\n        \n    def _organize_documents(self, input_folder: Path, output_base: Path, dry_run: bool) -> List[OrganizationResult]:\n        \"\"\"Organize document files.\"\"\"\n        results = []\n        document_files = self._discover_files(input_folder, ['.pdf', '.docx', '.txt', '.md'])\n        \n        for doc_file in document_files:\n            try:\n                result = self.document_processor.process_document(doc_file)\n                \n                if result['success'] and not dry_run:\n                    new_path = self._move_file(\n                        doc_file, \n                        output_base / \"documents\",\n                        result['new_filename'] + doc_file.suffix\n                    )\n                    \n                    results.append(OrganizationResult(\n                        original_path=doc_file,\n                        new_path=new_path,\n                        file_type='document',\n                        success=True,\n                        processing_time=result['processing_time'],\n                        analysis_data=result\n                    ))\n                elif dry_run:\n                    results.append(OrganizationResult(\n                        original_path=doc_file,\n                        new_path=output_base / \"documents\" / (result['new_filename'] + doc_file.suffix),\n                        file_type='document',\n                        success=True,\n                        processing_time=result['processing_time'],\n                        analysis_data=result\n                    ))\n                    \n            except Exception as e:\n                self.logger.error(f\"Failed to organize document {doc_file}: {e}\")\n                results.append(OrganizationResult(\n                    original_path=doc_file,\n                    new_path=Path(),\n                    file_type='document',\n                    success=False,\n                    error=str(e)\n                ))\n                \n        return results\n        \n    def _organize_audio(self, input_folder: Path, output_base: Path, dry_run: bool) -> List[OrganizationResult]:\n        \"\"\"Organize audio files.\"\"\"\n        results = []\n        audio_files = self._discover_files(input_folder, ['.mp3', '.wav', '.m4a', '.flac'])\n        \n        for audio_file in audio_files:\n            try:\n                result = Exception as e:\n                self.logger.error(f\"Failed to organize audio {audio_file}: {e}\")\n                results.append(OrganizationResult(\n                    original_path=audio_file,\n                    new_path=Path(),\n                    file_type='audio', \n                    success=False,\n                    error=str(e)\n                ))\n                \n        return results\n        \n    def _organize_video(self, input_folder: Path, output_base: Path, dry_run: bool) -> List[OrganizationResult]:\n        \"\"\"Organize video files.\"\"\"\n        results = []\n self.av_processor.process_media_file(video_file)\n                \n                if result['success'] and not dry_run:\n                    new_path = self._move_file(\n                        video_file,\n                        output_base / \"video\",\n                        result['new_filename'] + video_file.suffix\n                    )\n                    \n                    results.append(OrganizationResult(\n                        original_path=video_file,\n                        new_path=new_path,\n                        file_type='video',\n in extensions:\n            files.extend(folder.rglob(f\"*{ext}\"))\n            files.extend(folder.rglob(f\"*{ext.upper()}\"))\n        return files\n        \n    def _move_file(self, original: Path, target_dir: Path, new_filename: str) -> Path:\n        \"\"\"Move file to new location with conflict resolution.\"\"\"\n        target_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n        new_path = target_dir / new_filename\n        \n        # Handle duplicates\n        counter = 1\n        while new_path.exists():\n            name_part = new_path.stem\n            extension = new_path.suffix\n            new_path = target_dir / f\"{name_part}_{counter}{extension}\"\n            counter += 1\n            \n        original.rename(new_path)\n        return new_path\n        \n    def generate_report(self, results: List[OrganizationResult], output_path: Path):\n        \"\"\"Generate comprehensive organization report.\"\"\"\n        report = {\n            'summary': {\n                'total_files': len(results),\n                'successful': sum(1 for r in results if r.success),\n                'failed': sum(1 for r in results if not r.success),\n                'by_type': {}\n            },\n            'details': []\n        }\n        \n        # Calculate statistics by file type\n        for result in results:\n            file_type = result.file_type\n            if file_type not in report['summary']['by_type']:\n                report['summary']['by_type'][file_type] = {'total': 0, 'successful': 0}\n                \n            report['summary']['by_type'][file_type]['total'] += 1\n            if result.success:\n                report['summary']['by_type'][file_type]['successful'] += 1\n                \n            report['details'].append({\n                'original_path': str(result.original_path),\n                'new_path': str(result.new_path) if result.success else None,\n                'file_type': result.file_type,\n                'success': result.success,\n                'error': result.error,\n                'processing_time': result.processing_time\n            })\n            \n        # Save report\n        with open(output_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            json.dump(report, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n            \n        self.logger.info(f\"Organization report saved to: {output_path}\")\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Main entry point for unified organizer.\"\"\"\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description=\"Unified File Organization System\")\n    parser.add_argument(\"input_folder\", type=Path, help=\"Folder to organize\")\n    parser.add_argument(\"-o\", \"--output\", type=Path, help=\"Output base folder\")\n    parser.add_argument(\"--file-types\", nargs=\"+\", \n                       choices=['images', 'documents', 'audio', 'video'],\n                       default=['images', 'documents', 'audio', 'video'],\n                       help=\"File types to organize\")\n    parser.add_argument(\"--dry-run\", action=\"store_true\", help=\"Simulate without moving files\")\n organizer.logger.info(f\"Organization complete: {successful}/{len(results)} files processed successfully\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n```\n\n## 🚀 Usage"
