```json
            "type": "RESPONSE",
            "content": "I'll create a comprehensive bash script that opens API registration links and helps auto-fill/update your `.env` file with missing API keys.\n\n## 🔧 API Key Setup Assistant Script\n\n**`setup_missing_apis.sh`**\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n\n# =============================================================================\n# API Key Setup Assistant\n# =============================================================================\n# This script helps set up missing API keys by opening registration links\n# and providing guidance for updating your ~/.env file automatically.\n\nset -e\n\n# Colors for output\nRED='\\033[0;31m'\nGREEN='\\033[0;32m'\nYELLOW='\\033[1;33m'\nBLUE='\\033[0;34m'\nPURPLE='\\033[0;35m'\nCYAN='\\033[0;36m'\nNC='\\033[0m' # No Color\n\n# Logging functions\nlog_info() { echo -e \"${BLUE}[INFO]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_success() { echo -e \"${GREEN}[SUCCESS]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_warning() { echo -e \"${YELLOW}[WARNING]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_error() { echo -e \"${RED}[ERROR]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_api() { echo -e \"${PURPLE}[API]${NC} $1\"; }\nlog_step() { echo -e \"${CYAN}[STEP]${NC} $1\"; }\n\n# API configuration database\ndeclare -A API_DATABASE=(\n    # LLMs / TEXT / RESEARCH\n    [\"OPENAI_API_KEY\"]=\"OpenAI|https://platform.openai.com/api-keys\"\n    [\"ANTHROPIC_API_KEY\"]=\"Anthropic|https://console.anthropic.com/settings/keys\"\n    [\"PERPLEXITY_API_KEY\"]=\"Perplexity|https://www.perplexity.ai/settings/api\"\n    [\"XAI_API_KEY\"]=\"xAI|https://console.x.ai/\"\n    [\"GROQ_API_KEY\"]=\"Groq|https://console.groq.com/keys\"\n    [\"GEMINI_API_KEY\"]=\"Google Gemini|https://aistudio.google.com/app/apikey\"\n    \n    # ART / VISION / IMAGE\n    [\"IMAGGA_API_KEY\"]=\"Imagga|https://imagga.com/profile/keys\"\n    [\"IMAGGA_API_SECRET\"]=\"Imagga Secret|https://imagga.com/profile/keys\"\n    [\"IDEOGRAM_API_KEY\"]=\"Ideogram|https://ideogram.ai/api\"\n    [\"HUGGINGFACE_API_KEY\"]=\"HuggingFace|https://huggingface.co/settings/tokens\"\n    \n    # AUDIO / MUSIC / VIDEO\n    [\"ASSEMBLYAI_API_KEY\"]=\"AssemblyAI|https://www.assemblyai.com/app/account\"\n    [\"ELEVENLABS_API_KEY\"]=\"ElevenLabs|https://elevenlabs.io/speech-synthesis\"\n    [\"DEEPGRAM_API_KEY\"]=\"Deepgram|https://console.deepgram.com/signup\"\n    \n    # AUTOMATION / AGENTS / VECTOR DB\n    [\"FIREWORKS_API_KEY\"]=\"Fireworks AI|https://fireworks.ai/account/api-keys\"\n    [\"PINECONE_API_KEY\"]=\"Pinecone|https://www.pinecone.io/\"\n    [\"SUPABASE_KEY\"]=\"Supabase|https://supabase.com/dashboard/settings/api\"\n    [\"QDRANT_API_KEY\"]=\"Qdrant|https://cloud.qdrant.io/\"\n    [\"OPENROUTER_API_KEY\"]=\"OpenRouter|https://openrouter.ai/keys\"\n    [\"LANGSMITH_API_KEY\"]=\"LangSmith|https://smith.langchain.com/settings\"\n    \n    # CLOUD / INFRASTRUCTURE\n    [\"AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID\"]=\"AWS Access Key|https://us-east-1.console.aws.amazon.com/iam/home#/security_credentials\"\n    [\"AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY\"]=\"AWS Secret Key|https://us-east-1.console.aws.amazon.com/iam/home#/security_credentials\"\n    \n    # NETWORK / TUNNELING / DEVTOOLS\n    [\"NGROK_AUTHTOKEN\"]=\"Ngrok Auth Token|https://dashboard.ngrok.com/get-started/your-authtoken\"\n    [\"NGROK_API_KEY\"]=\"Ngrok API Key|https://dashboard.ngrok.com/api\"\n    \n    # OTHER SERVICES\n    [\"TAVILY_API_KEY\"]=\"Tavily|https://tavily.com/\"\n    [\"SERPAPI_KEY\"]=\"SerpAPI|https://serpapi.com/manage-api-key\"\n    [\"NEWSAPI_KEY\"]=\"NewsAPI|https://newsapi.org/register\"\n    [\"TWILIO_ACCOUNT_SID\"]=\"Twilio SID|https://www.twilio.com/console\"\n    [\"TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN\"]=\"Twilio Token|https://www.twilio.com/console\"\n    [\"NOTION_TOKEN\"]=\"Notion|https://www.notion.so/my-integrations\"\n)\n\n# Print banner\nprint_banner() {\n    echo\n    log_success \"╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗\"\n    log_success \"║                 API Key Setup Assistant                     ║\"\n    log_success \"║               Auto-configure Missing APIs                   ║\"\n    log_success \"╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝\"\n    echo\n}\n\n# Check if .env file exists\ncheck_env_file() {\n    local env_file=\"$HOME/.env\"\n    \n    if [[ ! -f \"$env_file\" ]]; then\n        log_warning \"No .env file found at $env_file\"\n        log_info \"Creating new .env file...\"\n        \n        # Create basic .env structure\n        cat > \"$env_file\" << 'ENV_HEADER'\n# =======================\n# 🌐 LLMs / TEXT / RESEARCH\n# =======================\n\n# =======================\n# 🖼️ ART / VISION / IMAGE  \n# =======================\n\n# =======================\n# 🎵 AUDIO / MUSIC / VIDEO\n# =======================\n\n# =======================\n# 🤖 AUTOMATION / AGENTS / VECTOR DB\n# =======================\n\n# =======================\n# ☁️ CLOUD / INFRASTRUCTURE\n# =======================\n\n# =======================\n# NETWORK / TUNNELING / DEVTOOLS\n# =======================\n\n# =======================\n# OTHER SERVICES\n# =======================\nENV_HEADER\n        \n        log_success \"Created new .env file at $env_file\"\n    else\n        log_success \"Found existing .env file at $env_file\"\n    fi\n    \n    echo \"$env_file\"\n}\n\n# Parse current .env file and extract existing keys\nparse_existing_keys() {\n    local env_file=\"$1\"\n    declare -A existing_keys\n    \n    if [[ -f \"$env_file\" ]]; then\n        while IFS='=' read -r key value || [[ -n \"$key\" ]]; do\n            # Skip comments and empty lines\n            if [[ $key =~ ^[[:space:]]*# ]] || [[ -z \"$key\" ]]; then\n                continue\n            fi\n            # Remove leading/trailing whitespace\n            key=$(echo \"$key\" | xargs)\n            value=$(echo \"$value\" | xargs)\n            existing_keys[\"$key\"]=\"$value\"\n        done < \"$env_file\"\n    fi\n    \n    # Return the associative array\n    for key in \"${!existing_keys[@]}\"; do\n        echo \"$key|${existing_keys[$key]}\"\n    done\n}\n\n# Detect missing API keys\nfind_missing_keys() {\n    local env_file=\"$1\"\n    declare -a missing_keys\n    \n    # Parse existing keys\n    declare -A existing_keys\n    while IFS='|' read -r key value; do\n        existing_keys[\"$key\"]=\"$value\"\n    done < <(parse_existing_keys \"$env_file\")\n    \n    # Check each API in our database\n    for api_key in \"${!API_DATABASE[@]}\"; do\n        if [[ -z \"${existing_keys[$api_key]}\" ]]; then\n            missing_keys+=(\"$api_key\")\n        elif [[ \"${existing_keys[$api_key]}\" == \"\" ]]; then\n            missing_keys+=(\"$api_key\")\n        fi\n    done\n    \n    printf '%s\\n' \"${missing_keys[@]}\"\n}\n\n# Open browser to API registration page\nopen_api_registration() {\n    local api_key=\"$1\"\n    local api_info=\"${API_DATABASE[$api_key]}\"\n    \n    if [[ -n \"$api_info\" ]]; then\n        IFS='|' read -r service_name registration_url <<< \"$api_info\"\n        log_api \"Opening $service_name registration: $registration_url\"\n        \n        # Open in default browser\n        if command -v open >/dev/null 2>&1; then\n            # macOS\n            open \"$registration_url\"\n        elif command -v xdg-open >/dev/null 2>&1; then\n            # Linux\n            xdg-open \"$registration_url\"\n        elif command -v start >/dev/null 2>&1; then\n            # Windows (if using WSL)\n            start \"$registration_url\"\n        else\n            log_warning \"Could not automatically open browser. Please visit: $registration_url\"\n        fi\n    else\n        log_warning \"No registration URL found for $api_key\"\n    fi\n}\n\n# Interactive API key input\nget_api_key_interactive() {\n    local api_key=\"$1\"\n    local api_info=\"${API_DATABASE[$api_key]}\"\n    IFS='|' read -r service_name registration_url <<< \"$api_info\"\n    \n    echo\n    log_step \"Setting up: $service_name ($api_key)\"\n    log_info \"Registration URL: $registration_url\"\n    \n    # Open browser if user wants\n    read -p \"Open registration page in browser? (y/N): \" -n 1 -r\n    echo\n    if [[ $REPLY =~ ^[Yy]$ ]]; then\n        open_api_registration \"$api_key\"\n    fi\n    \n    # Get API key from user\n    while true; do\n        read -p \"Enter your $service_name API key: \" api_value\n        if [[ -n \"$api_value\" ]]; then\n            echo \"$api_value\"\n            break\n        else\n            log_warning \"API key cannot be empty. Press Ctrl+C to skip this API.\"\n        fi\n    done\n}\n\n# Auto-detect API key format and provide hints\nprovide_api_hints() {\n    local api_key=\"$1\"\n    \n    case \"$api_key\" in\n        \"OPENAI_API_KEY\")\n            log_info \"💡 Hint: OpenAI keys start with 'sk-' and are 51 characters long\"\n            ;;\n        \"ANTHROPIC_API_KEY\")\n            log_info \"💡 Hint: Anthropic keys start with 'sk-ant-' and are ~100 characters\"\n            ;;\n        \"AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID\")\n            log_info \"💡 Hint: AWS Access Key ID starts with 'AKIA' and is 20 characters\"\n            ;;\n        \"AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY\")\n            log_info \"💡 Hint: AWS Secret Access Key is 40 characters long\"\n            ;;\n        \"NGROK_AUTHTOKEN\")\n            log_info \"💡 Hint: Ngrok auth token starts with '2' and is ~40 characters\"\n            ;;\n        \"ELEVENLABS_API_KEY\")\n            log_info \"💡 Hint: ElevenLabs keys are long alphanumeric strings\"\n            ;;\n        \"NOTION_TOKEN\")\n            log_info \"💡 Hint: Notion tokens start with 'secret_'\"\n            ;;\n    esac\n}\n\n# Update .env file with new API key\nupdate_env_file() {\n    local env_file=\"$1\"\n    local api_key=\"$2\"\n    local api_value=\"$3\"\n    \n    # Backup original file\n    cp \"$env_file\" \"$env_file.backup.$(date +%s)\"\n    \n    # Check if key already exists (empty or commented)\n    if grep -q \"^[[:space:]]*$api_key=\" \"$env_file\"; then\n        # Key exists, update it\n        if [[ \"$OSTYPE\" == \"darwin\"* ]]; then\n            # macOS\n            sed -i '' \"s|^[[:space:]]*$api_key=.*|$api_key=$api_value|\" \"$env_file\"\n        else\n            # Linux\n            sed -i \"s|^[[:space:]]*$api_key=.*|$api_key=$api_value|\" \"$env_file\"\n        fi\n        log_success \"Updated $api_key in .env file\"\n    else\n        # Key doesn't exist, add it in appropriate section\n        local section=\"\"\n        case \"$api_key\" in\n            OPENAI*|ANTHROPIC*|PERPLEXITY*|XAI*|GROQ*|GEMINI*)\n                section=\"🌐 LLMs / TEXT / RESEARCH\"\n                ;;\n            IMAGGA*|IDEOGRAM*|HUGGINGFACE*)\n                section=\"🖼️ ART / VISION / IMAGE\"\n                ;;\n            ASSEMBLYAI*|ELEVENLABS*|DEEPGRAM*)\n                section=\"🎵 AUDIO / MUSIC / VIDEO\"\n                ;;\n            FIREWORKS*|PINECONE*|SUPABASE*|QDRANT*|OPENROUTER*|LANGSMITH*)\n                section=\"🤖 AUTOMATION / AGENTS / VECTOR DB\"\n                ;;\n            AWS*)\n                section=\"☁️ CLOUD / INFRASTRUCTURE\"\n                ;;\n            NGROK*)\n                section=\"NETWORK / TUNNELING / DEVTOOLS\"\n                ;;\n            TAVILY*|SERPAPI*|NEWSAPI*|TWILIO*|NOTION*)\n                section=\"OTHER SERVICES\"\n                ;;\n            *)\n                section=\"OTHER SERVICES\"\n                ;;\n        esac\n        \n        # Add the key after the section header\n        if [[ \"$OSTYPE\" == \"darwin\"* ]]; then\n            # macOS\n            sed -i '' \"/^# =======================$/{\nN\n/# $section$/a\\\\\n$api_key=$api_value\n}\" \"$env_file\"\n        else\n            # Linux\n            sed -i \"/^# =======================$/{\nN\n/# $section$/a\\\\\n$api_key=$api_value\n}\" \"$env_file\"\n        fi\n        \n        log_success \"Added $api_key to .env file in $section section\"\n    fi\n}\n\n# Batch setup for multiple APIs\nsetup_multiple_apis() {\n    local env_file=\"$1\"\n    shift\n    local apis=(\"$@\")\n    \n    for api_key in \"${apis[@]}\"; do\n        provide_api_hints \"$api_key\"\n        local api_value\n        api_value=$(get_api_key_interactive \"$api_key\")\n        update_env_file \"$env_file\" \"$api_key\" \"$api_value\"\n    done\n}\n\n# Show current API key status\nshow_api_status() {\n    local env_file=\"$1\"\n    \n    log_step \"Current API Key Status:\"\n    echo\n    \n    # Parse existing keys\n    declare -A existing_keys\n    while IFS='|' read -r key value; do\n        existing_keys[\"$key\"]=\"$value\"\n    done < <(parse_existing_keys \"$env_file\")\n    \n    # Check each API\n    local total=0\n    local configured=0\n    \n    for category in \"🌐 LLMs / TEXT / RESEARCH\" \"🖼️ ART / VISION / IMAGE\" \"🎵 AUDIO / MUSIC / VIDEO\" \"🤖 AUTOMATION / AGENTS / VECTOR DB\" \"☁️ CLOUD / INFRASTRUCTURE\" \"NETWORK / TUNNELING / DEVTOOLS\" \"OTHER SERVICES\"; do\n        echo \"${BLUE}$category${NC}\"\n        \n        for api_key in \"${!API_DATABASE[@]}\"; do\n            local api_info=\"${API_DATABASE[$api_key]}\"\n            IFS='|' read -r service_name registration_url <<< \"$api_info\"\n            \n            # Determine category\n            local api_category=\"\"\n            case \"$api_key\" in\n                OPENAI*|ANTHROPIC*|PERPLEXITY*|XAI*|GROQ*|GEMINI*) api_category=\"🌐 LLMs / TEXT / RESEARCH\" ;;\n                IMAGGA*|IDEOGRAM*|HUGGINGFACE*) api_category=\"🖼️ ART / VISION / IMAGE\" ;;\n                ASSEMBLYAI*|ELEVENLABS*|DEEPGRAM*) api_category=\"🎵 AUDIO / MUSIC / VIDEO\" ;;\n                FIREWORKS*|PINECONE*|SUPABASE*|QDRANT*|OPENROUTER*|LANGSMITH*) api_category=\"🤖 AUTOMATION / AGENTS / VECTOR DB\" ;;\n                AWS*) api_category=\"☁️ CLOUD / INFRASTRUCTURE\" ;;\n                NGROK*) api_category=\"NETWORK / TUNNELING / DEVTOOLS\" ;;\n                *) api_category=\"OTHER SERVICES\" ;;\n            esac\n            \n            if [[ \"$api_category\" == \"$category\" ]]; then\n                total=$((total + 1))\n                if [[ -n \"${existing_keys[$api_key]}\" && \"${existing_keys[$api_key]}\" != \"\" ]]; then\n                    echo \"  ✅ $service_name: ${GREEN}Configured${NC}\"\n                    configured=$((configured + 1))\n                else\n                    echo \"  ❌ $service_name: ${RED}Missing${NC}\"\n                fi\n            fi\n        done\n        echo\n    done\n    \n    local percentage=$((configured * 100 / total))\n    log_info \"Progress: $configured/$total APIs configured ($percentage%)\"\n    echo\n}\n\n# Main interactive setup function\ninteractive_setup() {\n    local env_file\n    env_file=$(check_env_file)\n    \n    while true; do\n        echo\n        log_step \"API Setup Menu\"\n        echo \"1. Show current API status\"\n        echo \"2. Setup all missing APIs\"\n        echo \"3. Setup specific API category\"\n        echo \"4. Setup individual API\"\n        echo \"5. Validate current API keys\"\n        echo \"6. Exit\"\n        echo\n        \n        read -p \"Choose an option (1-6): \" choice\n        \n        case $choice in\n            1)\n                show_api_status \"$env_file\"\n                ;;\n            2)\n                log_step \"Setting up all missing APIs...\"\n                local missing_keys\n                mapfile -t missing_keys < <(find_missing_keys \"$env_file\")\n                \n                if [[ ${#missing_keys[@]} -eq 0 ]]; then\n                    log_success \"All APIs are already configured!\"\n                else\n                    log_info \"Found ${#missing_keys[@]} missing APIs\"\n                    setup_multiple_apis \"$env_file\" \"${missing_keys[@]}\"\n                fi\n                ;;\n            3)\n                setup_by_category \"$env_file\"\n                ;;\n            4)\n                setup_individual_api \"$env_file\"\n                ;;\n            5)\n                validate_api_keys \"$env_file\"\n                ;;\n            6)\n                log_success \"Exiting API Setup Assistant\"\n                exit 0\n                ;;\n            *)\n                log_error \"Invalid option. Please choose 1-6.\"\n                ;;\n        esac\n    done\n}\n\n# Setup by category\nsetup_by_category() {\n    local env_file=\"$1\"\n    \n    echo\n    log_step \"Select API Category:\"\n    echo \"1. 🌐 LLMs / TEXT / RESEARCH\"\n    echo \"2. 🖼️ ART / VISION / IMAGE\"\n    echo \"3. 🎵 AUDIO / MUSIC / VIDEO\"\n    echo \"4. 🤖 AUTOMATION / AGENTS / VECTOR DB\"\n    echo \"5. ☁️ CLOUD / INFRASTRUCTURE\"\n    echo \"6. NETWORK / TUNNELING / DEVTOOLS\"\n    echo \"7. OTHER SERVICES\"\n    echo \"8. Back to main menu\"\n    echo\n    \n    read -p \"Choose category (1-8): \" category_choice\n    \n    case $category_choice in\n        1) category=\"🌐 LLMs / TEXT / RESEARCH\" ;;\n        2) category=\"🖼️ ART / VISION / IMAGE\" ;;\n        3) category=\"🎵 AUDIO / MUSIC / VIDEO\" ;;\n        4) category=\"🤖 AUTOMATION / AGENTS / VECTOR DB\" ;;\n        5) category=\"☁️ CLOUD / INFRASTRUCTURE\" ;;\n        6) category=\"NETWORK / TUNNELING / DEVTOOLS\" ;;\n        7) category=\"OTHER SERVICES\" ;;\n        8) return ;;\n        *) log_error \"Invalid choice\"; return ;;\n    esac\n    \n    # Find APIs in this category\n    declare -a category_apis=()\n    for api_key in \"${!API_DATABASE[@]}\"; do\n        local api_category=\"\"\n        case \"$api_key\" in\n            OPENAI*|ANTHROPIC*|PERPLEXITY*|XAI*|GROQ*|GEMINI*) api_category=\"🌐 LLMs / TEXT / RESEARCH\" ;;\n            IMAGGA*|IDEOGRAM*|HUGGINGFACE*) api_category=\"🖼️ ART / VISION / IMAGE\" ;;\n            ASSEMBLYAI*|ELEVENLABS*|DEEPGRAM*) api_category=\"🎵 AUDIO / MUSIC / VIDEO\" ;;\n            FIREWORKS*|PINECONE*|SUPABASE*|QDRANT*|OPENROUTER*|LANGSMITH*) api_category=\"🤖 AUTOMATION / AGENTS / VECTOR DB\" ;;\n            AWS*) api_category=\"☁️ CLOUD / INFRASTRUCTURE\" ;;\n            NGROK*) api_category=\"NETWORK / TUNNELING / DEVTOOLS\" ;;\n            *) api_category=\"OTHER SERVICES\" ;;\n        esac\n        \n        if [[ \"$api_category\" == \"$category\" ]]; then\n            category_apis+=(\"$api_key\")\n        fi\n    done\n    \n    # Check which ones are missing\n    declare -a missing_in_category=()\n    for api_key in \"${category_apis[@]}\"; do\n        if ! grep -q \"^[[:space:]]*$api_key=.*\" \"$env_file\" || grep -q \"^[[:space:]]*$api_key=[[:space:]]*$\" \"$env_file\"; then\n            missing_in_category+=(\"$api_key\")\n        fi\n    done\n    \n    if [[ ${#missing_in_category[@]} -eq 0 ]]; then\n        log_success \"All APIs in $category are already configured!\"\n    else\n        log_info \"Found ${#missing_in_category[@]} missing APIs in $category\"\n        setup_multiple_apis \"$env_file\" \"${missing_in_category[@]}\"\n    fi\n}\n\n# Setup individual API\nsetup_individual_api() {\n    local env_file=\"$1\"\n    \n    echo\n    log_step \"Available APIs:\"\n    local i=1\n    declare -a api_list\n    for api_key in \"${!API_DATABASE[@]}\"; do\n        local api_info=\"${API_DATABASE[$api_key]}\"\n        IFS='|' read -r service_name registration_url <<< \"$api_info\"\n        echo \"$i. $service_name ($api_key)\"\n        api_list[$i]=\"$api_key\"\n        i=$((i + 1))\n    done\n    echo \"$i. Back to main menu\"\n    echo\n    \n    read -p \"Choose API (1-$i): \" api_choice\n    \n    if [[ $api_choice -eq $i ]]; then\n        return\n    elif [[ $api_choice -ge 1 && $api_choice -lt $i ]]; then\n        local selected_api=\"${api_list[$api_choice]}\"\n        provide_api_hints \"$selected_api\"\n        local api_value\n        api_value=$(get_api_key_interactive \"$selected_api\")\n        update_env_file \"$env_file\" \"$selected_api\" \"$api_value\"\n    else\n        log_error \"Invalid choice\"\n    fi\n}\n\n# Validate API keys (basic format checking)\nvalidate_api_keys() {\n    local env_file=\"$1\"\n    log_step \"Validating API keys...\"\n    \n    # Parse existing keys\n    declare -A existing_keys\n    while IFS='|' read -r key value; do\n        existing_keys[\"$key\"]=\"$value\"\n    done < <(parse_existing_keys \"$env_file\")\n    \n    local valid_count=0\n    local total_checked=0\n    \n    for api_key in \"${!existing_keys[@]}\"; do\n        local value=\"${existing_keys[$api_key]}\"\n        \n        if [[ -n \"$value\" ]]; then\n            total_checked=$((total_checked + 1))\n            \n            case \"$api_key\" in\n                \"OPENAI_API_KEY\")\n                    if [[ \"$value\" =~ ^sk-[a-zA-Z0-9]{48}$ ]]; then\n                        echo \"✅ $api_key: Valid format\"\n                        valid_count=$((valid_count + 1))\n                    else\n                        echo \"❌ $api_key: Invalid format (should start with 'sk-' and be 51 chars)\"\n                    fi\n                    ;;\n                \"AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID\")\n                    if [[ \"$value\" =~ ^AKIA[0-9A-Z]{16}$ ]]; then\n                        echo \"✅ $api_key: Valid format\"\n                        valid_count=$((valid_count + 1))\n                    else\n                        echo \"❌ $api_key: Invalid format (should start with 'AKIA' and be 20 chars)\"\n                    fi\n                    ;;\n                \"NGROK_AUTHTOKEN\")\n                    if [[ \"$value\" =~ ^2[a-zA-Z0-9_]{35,}$ ]]; then\n                        echo \"✅ $api_key: Valid format\"\n                        valid_count=$((valid_count + 1))\n                    else\n                        echo \"❌ $api_key: Invalid format (should start with '2' and be ~40 chars)\"\n                    fi\n                    ;;\n                *)\n                    echo \"✅ $api_key: Present\"\n                    valid_count=$((valid_count + 1))\n                    ;;\n            esac\n        fi\n    done\n    \n    if [[ $total_checked -gt 0 ]]; then\n        local validation_rate=$((valid_count * 100 / total_checked))\n        log_info \"Validation: $valid_count/$total_checked keys valid ($validation_rate%)\"\n    else\n        log_warning \"No API keys found to validate\"\n    fi\n}\n\n# Quick setup mode (non-interactive)\nquick_setup() {\n    local env_file\n    env_file=$(check_env_file)\n    \n    log_step \"Quick Setup Mode\"\n    show_api_status \"$env_file\"\n    \n    local missing_keys\n    mapfile -t missing_keys < <(find_missing_keys \"$env_file\")\n    \n    if [[ ${#missing_keys[@]} -eq 0 ]]; then\n        log_success \"All APIs are already configured!\"\n        exit 0\n    fi\n    \n    log_info \"Found ${#missing_keys[@]} missing APIs\"\n    echo\n    \n    for api_key in \"${missing_keys[@]}\"; do\n        local api_info=\"${API_DATABASE[$api_key]}\"\n        IFS='|' read -r service_name registration_url <<< \"$api_info\"\n        \n        log_step \"Setting up: $service_name\"\n        log_info \"Registration: $registration_url\"\n        open_api_registration \"$api_key\"\n        \n        read -p \"Enter your $service_name API key (or press Enter to skip): \" api_value\n        \n        if [[ -n \"$api_value\" ]]; then\n            update_env_file \"$env_file\" \"$api_key\" \"$api_value\"\n            log_success \"✅ $service_name configured\"\n        else\n            log_warning \"⏭️  Skipped $service_name\"\n        fi\n        echo\n    done\n    \n    show_api_status \"$env_file\"\n}\n\n# Main function\nmain() {\n    print_banner\n    \n    # Check for command line arguments\n    if [[ \"$1\" == \"--quick\" ]] || [[ \"$1\" == \"-q\" ]]; then\n        quick_setup\n    elif [[ \"$1\" == \"--validate\" ]] || [[ \"$1\" == \"-v\" ]]; then\n        env_file=$(check_env_file)\n        validate_api_keys \"$env_file\"\n    elif [[ \"$1\" == \"--status\" ]] || [[ \"$1\" == \"-s\" ]]; then\n        env_file=$(check_env_file)\n        show_api_status \"$env_file\"\n    else\n        interactive_setup\n    fi\n}\n\n# Run main function\nmain \"$@\"\n```\n\n## 🚀 Usage Instructions\n\n1. **Make the script executable:**\n   ```bash\n   chmod +x setup_missing_apis.sh\n   ```\n\n2. **Run in interactive mode (recommended):**\n   ```bash\n   ./setup_missing_apis.sh\n   ```\n\n3. **Or use quick setup:**\n   ```bash\n   ./setup_missing_apis.sh --quick\n   ```\n\n4. **Check current status:**\n   ```bash\n   ./setup_missing_apis.sh --status\n   ```\n\n5. **Validate existing keys:**\n   ```bash\n   ./setup_missing_apis.sh --validate\n   ```\n\n## 🎯 Features\n\n### 🔍 **Automatic Detection**\n- Scans your `~/.env` file for missing API keys\n- Categorizes APIs by type (LLMs, Vision, Audio, etc.)\n- Shows progress and completion status\n\n### 🌐 **Smart Registration**\n- Opens correct registration pages in your browser\n- Provides hints about expected key formats\n- Covers 30+ different AI APIs and services\n\n### ⚡ **Auto-Update**\n- Intelligently updates your `.env` file\n- Preserves existing configurations\n- Organizes keys in proper sections\n- Creates backups before modifications\n\n### 🛡️ **Validation**\n- Basic format validation for common APIs\n- Checks for empty or malformed keys\n- Provides feedback on configuration quality\n\n### 📊 **Progress Tracking**\n- Visual progress indicators\n- Category-based organization\n- Completion percentages\n\nThe script will guide you through setting up all your missing APIs, open the correct registration pages, and automatically update your `.env` file with the proper formatting!"
          }
        ]
      }
    }
  }
}
```
